id='poem_sentence_1_163615'>江山旧是无诸国，楼殿今为极乐天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163615'>五马如君多暇少，一樽惟我共游偏。<div class='inlineComment2'>（自注：洞中有老僧。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163556'>龙台日上千峰出，雁塔云生一径迷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163556'>知有岭猿犹在否，使君高卧莫教啼<span class='inlineComment2'>（五字原缺，据四库本补）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163555'>猿惊出洞时三哭<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作器，据清钞本、四库本改）</span>，梅送行人早一番。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163555'>此去蓬莱峰顶月，梦魂应到荔枝园。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/163638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郊祀庆成诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163638")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163638'>皇帝即位，厉精求治。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163638'>翼翼兢兢，以畏天异。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163638'>乃见宗庙，乃严郊祭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163638'>赫赫烈祖，陟配上帝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163638'>皇帝肇祀，心虔诚至。<div id='poem_sentence_4_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_163638'>斋居撤膳，夙兴弗寐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_163638'>不履黄道，不御小次。<div id='poem_sentence_6_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_163638'>出宿于庙，阴雨翳翳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_163638'>既其徂郊，日出晰晰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_163638'>登丘奏假，天地澄霁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_163638'>礼终乐阕，神贶来暨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_163638'>皇帝还跸，千乘万骑。<div id='poem_sentence_11_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_163638'>雷动天旋，臣民欣慰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_163638'>御楼肆赦，躬册丹地。<div id='poem_sentence_13_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_163638'>恩流泽洽，周匝无际。<div id='poem_sentence_14_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_163638'>惟诚感神，惟德销沴。<div id='poem_sentence_15_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_163638'>皇帝能飨，时赐坐致。<div id='poem_sentence_16_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_163638'>臣愿皇帝，事天寅畏。<div id='poem_sentence_17_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_163638'>左右惟贤，安民惟惠。<div id='poem_sentence_18_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_163638'>无咈忠谏，无轻政事。<div id='poem_sentence_19_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_163638'>日新一日，庶答天意。<div id='poem_sentence_20_163638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_163638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_163638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　陈襄撰《吴君唐卿墓志铭》<div id='poem_1169573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴君唐卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169573")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169573'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169573'>君讳辅尧，字唐卿，建之浦城人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169573_comment'></div>庆历中，予为县主簿，有吴生道者来学于予，年方十数岁，而好古有志，即君之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169573_comment'></div>予官浦城三年，衣冠大姓有以事渎于官者，常无虚日，而君在乡閒居谨畏，其足迹未尝一蹑公门，君之为人可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169573_comment'></div>皇祐四年，予复过浦城，君趣令诸子走见，而道之文行益有可观，惜无师友以成之，将挈而西，与君相见，具道其事，君闻之，䜣然无难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169573_comment'></div>道既与予偕至京师，馆于河阳，后又肄业于太学，求试于礼部，舍亲之养凡八年，而君无一言以饬其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169573_comment'></div>视其子之于学，虽在数千里之外，其心安焉如在其左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169573_comment'></div>故君之亡四十馀日，而道始归而哭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169573_comment'></div>君之始家闽中，曾祖承蕴，仕五代，至显官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169573_comment'></div>祖仁凯，国初为广州新会县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169573_comment'></div>父朴，不仕，以刚直负气，为权贵者诬搆而卒于狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169573_comment'></div>君年甫及冠，无昆弟之亲，悼父非辜，激昂自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169573_comment'></div>治家事产业，奉母以孝，母且老，斯须不去其侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169573_comment'></div>稼穑辛勤，给于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169573_comment'></div>君为人资性谨重，奉身俭约，而与人周，不渔细民，不徇污俗，闻人有善则喜之，见人患难则戚戚若有疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169573_comment'></div>先有女兄适掌书记章铎，铎之殁，诸孤幼弱，君为之营置田庐以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169573_comment'></div>娶李氏，始终顺睦，及迎李氏之寡母徐氏，养之终身，葬送以礼，岁时不绝其祀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169573_comment'></div>君少以家难废学，颇自为恨，因力帅诸子，出就师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169573_comment'></div>岁计之入，惟供给嫁娶伏腊，自馀悉以与诸子为学之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169573_comment'></div>尝诲其子曰：「汝曹茍有一介之善，使吾耳闻目见，虽死无恨矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169573_comment'></div>故其子五人：长曰识者，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169573_comment'></div>其次曰诚，曰诩，曰道，曰详，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169573_comment'></div>而道尤有志节，能修身治性，将不为事物之惑，使之不已，必能有见于世，斯亦足以成君志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169573_comment'></div>女三人，长适李氏，其次皆适黄氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169573_comment'></div>孙十有一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169573_comment'></div>女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169573_comment'></div>享年七十有四，卜嘉祐四年冬十有二月十一日，葬于安仁乡龙兴里溪北社莲寺之西冈，从君之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169573_comment'></div>其子道论次君之行实，遣奴赍状如京师，见属为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169573_comment'></div>曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1169573'>莫生惟勤，令于其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169573_comment'></div>莫死为已，克昌厥子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169573_comment'></div>莲华之冈，式安以藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1169573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　陈襄著《中庸讲义》<div id='poem_1169562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>礼记讲议 中庸</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169562")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169562'>《中庸》者，治性之书，孔子之孙子思之所述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169562_comment'></div>自孔子没，性命之书无传，虽其说间见于六经，然辞约义微，学者难晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169562_comment'></div>故子思传其学于曾子，其间多引孔子之言，则是书祖述圣人理性之学，最为详备，使学者求之，足以知道德诚明之本焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169562_comment'></div>中者，性之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169562_comment'></div>庸者，性之用也，常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169562_comment'></div>人受天地之中以生，其性莫非善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169562_comment'></div>至中至正，以为民极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169562_comment'></div>其不善者，非性也，人之欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169562_comment'></div>故子思曰：「喜怒哀乐之未发，谓之中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169562_comment'></div>「中者，天下之大本是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169562_comment'></div>中之用有五，仁、义、礼、智、信是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169562_comment'></div>循是五者而行，则可以为万世常久不易之道，故曰中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1169562'>天命之谓性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1169562'>人生而静，情欲未发，其中湛然，则有恻隐之心存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169562_comment'></div>恻隐之心，仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169562_comment'></div>羞恶之心，义也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169562_comment'></div>恭逊之心，礼也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169562_comment'></div>是非之心，智也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169562_comment'></div>不欺之心，信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169562_comment'></div>惟是五者，不待学而后能，故曰天之所命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169562_comment'></div>是性也，与天地同出于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169562_comment'></div>道者先天地而有，《易》曰「形而上者谓之道」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169562_comment'></div>道有变化，故有气也，形也，性也，三者并立，而五材各具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169562_comment'></div>气升而上以为天，故有五星之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169562_comment'></div>形降而下以为地，故有五行之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169562_comment'></div>性命于两间以为人，故有五常之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169562_comment'></div>乾坤有四德以配五常：元者，在气为春，在形为木，在性为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169562_comment'></div>亨者，在气为夏，在形为火，在性为礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169562_comment'></div>利者，在气为秋，在形为金，在性为义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169562_comment'></div>贞者，在气为冬，在形为水，在性为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169562_comment'></div>乾坤不言智，而独命之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169562_comment'></div>故《易》曰：「君子行此四德者，故曰：『《乾》：元、亨、利、贞也』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169562_comment'></div>又《说卦》曰：「立天之道曰阴与阳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169562_comment'></div>以气言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169562_comment'></div>「立地之道曰柔与刚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169562_comment'></div>以形言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169562_comment'></div>「立人之道曰仁与义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169562_comment'></div>以性言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169562_comment'></div>「兼三才而两之，故《易》六画而成卦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169562_comment'></div>盖取乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169562_comment'></div>则是人之性与天地同出于道，而神于万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169562_comment'></div>凡有血气心知之类，统为之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169562_comment'></div>上自圣人生而知之，其次学而知之，及其至一也，高明博大，悠久不息，与天地并立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169562_comment'></div>可不尊乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1169562'>率性之谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1169562'>率，循也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169562_comment'></div>凡人之性未接于物，莫非善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169562_comment'></div>接于物而情生，则有喜、怒、哀、惧、爱、恶、欲七者形焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169562_comment'></div>故情有善有不善，以性行情，情则善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169562_comment'></div>《乾》卦曰：「利贞者，性情是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169562_comment'></div>以情盗性，情则恶矣，《记》曰「人化物者，灭天理而穷人欲」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169562_comment'></div>如此，则莫非不善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169562_comment'></div>人能循是五常之性而行，不为情欲之所迁夺，则其道常存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169562_comment'></div>故循之谓道，离之非道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1169562'>修道之谓教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1169562'>教，效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169562_comment'></div>圣人知人之性感物而迁，因其性之所自有，修而明之，以教天下，使人知所则效，而复归于道，夫是之谓教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169562_comment'></div>然则人之性无以异于圣人之性？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169562_comment'></div>圣人之性诚而不动，明而不惑，故情伪莫能迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169562_comment'></div>众人之性不胜其情，欲动乎内，物交乎外，不能以自反，其道遂亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169562_comment'></div>此所以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1169562_comment'></div>夫杀一不辜，人莫不恻然有所不忍，此天下之心同仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1169562_comment'></div>有是心而为不仁者，彼有以害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1169562_comment'></div>行一不义，人莫不恻然有所不为，此天下之心同义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1169562_comment'></div>有是心而为不义者，彼有以贼之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1169562_comment'></div>尊君而卑臣，隆父而杀子，此天下之心同礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1169562_comment'></div>有是心而为无礼者，彼有以慢之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1169562_comment'></div>是是而非非，好善而恶恶，此天下之心同智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1169562_comment'></div>有是心而为不智者，彼有以蔽之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1169562_comment'></div>内以欺诸己，外以欺诸人，则怍焉，此天下之心同信也，有是心而为不信者，彼有以迁之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1169562_comment'></div>故有之者性也，失之者情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1169562_comment'></div>不正其情，无以反其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1169562_comment'></div>如此者必待学而后明，修而后复，自致曲至于能化之谓修道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1169562_comment'></div>修者人之道，故谓之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1169562'>道也者，不可须臾离也，可离非道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1169562'>道者，得之天命之正，失于人欲之邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1169562_comment'></div>正与邪，君子小人之辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1169562_comment'></div>故君子须臾之间不可离于正道，离正适邪即非是道，故曰：「可离非道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1169562_comment'></div>孔子曰：「君子无终食之间违仁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1169562", 1169562, "Clauses/208/Comments/0")'>造次</span>必于是，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1169562", 1169562, "Clauses/209/Comments/1")'>颠沛</span>必于是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1169562_comment'></div>又曰：「人皆曰予智，择乎中庸，而不能期月守也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1169562_comment'></div>独称颜子「其心三月不违仁」，「择乎中庸，得一善，则拳拳服膺而弗失」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1169562_comment'></div>若颜子，可谓庶几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1169562_comment'></div>然则君子终身由于道，而不失于须臾之间，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1169562_comment'></div>非仁以任之，智以乐之，勇以决之，则不可能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1169562'>是故君子戒慎乎其所不睹，恐惧乎其所不闻，莫见乎隐，莫显乎微，故君子慎其独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1169562'>夫中庸之学，治心养性，必自于隐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1169562_comment'></div>如隐微之不正，而欲成圣人君子之德，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1169562_comment'></div>故君子之所养，在明乎性情善恶之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1169562_comment'></div>方其心之所生，性也，情也，不可不辨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1169562_comment'></div>吾所可欲，正而公者，善也，性也，吾择而守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1169562_comment'></div>吾所不欲，邪而私者，恶也，情也，吾拒而弗行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1169562_comment'></div>其所不睹，谓未形于行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1169562_comment'></div>其所不闻，谓未形于言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1169562_comment'></div>心之所生，不待形于言，行于其不睹不闻之际，常当戒慎恐惧，不使须臾之间情害其性，而离于道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1169562_comment'></div>闻见之不及，隐也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1169562_comment'></div>言动之未形，微也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1169562_comment'></div>众人之患，在于隐微之间，谓其不睹不闻而为不善，不知其发而不掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1169562_comment'></div>「莫见乎隐者」，谓隐而必见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1169562_comment'></div>「莫显乎微者」，谓微而必显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1169562_comment'></div>故君子閒居慎独，诚心养正，不敢以自欺，然后成其德性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_1169562'>喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中，发而皆中节，谓之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1169562_comment'></div>中也者，天下之大本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1169562_comment'></div>和也者，天下之达道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1169562_comment'></div>致中和，天地位焉，万物育焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1169562'>喜怒哀乐者非情也，中者性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1169562_comment'></div>人生则有性，有性则有情，情之未发，莫非性也，故谓之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1169562_comment'></div>发而本于中，莫非道也，故谓之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1169562_comment'></div>中之所有，仁、义、礼、智、信，非由外铄我者也，初是五者之端，若甚微而不可明，及其择而守之，扩而充之，则诚且明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1169562_comment'></div>诚至于不息，然后能定，有以尽天下之神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1169562_comment'></div>明至于不惑，然后能应，有以尽天下之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1169562_comment'></div>中至于如此，则大人之事备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1169562_comment'></div>故曰：「天下之大本也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1169562_comment'></div>和之所发，喜怒哀乐，人情之所不免者也，虽圣人不得而绝之，惟其正而不邪，公而不私，是以动而有节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1169562_comment'></div>喜非吾喜也，人喜则喜，故赏一善，人以为仁焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1169562_comment'></div>怒非吾怒也，人怒则怒，故刑一恶，人以为义焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1169562_comment'></div>喜以天下，怒以天下，此喜怒之中节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1169562_comment'></div>哀非吾哀也，人哀则哀，故为之丧纪之数，人以为礼焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1169562_comment'></div>乐非吾乐也，人乐则乐，故为雅颂之音，人以为乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1169562_comment'></div>哀以天下，乐以天下，此哀乐之中节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1169562_comment'></div>和至于如此，则天下之志得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1169562_comment'></div>故曰：「天下之达道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1169562_comment'></div>凡人之情皆可以致中和，然而不能者，以利欲害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1169562_comment'></div>惟圣人能致之，故可以赞天地之化育矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1169562_comment'></div>天地之道，以正为中，以利为和，而万物生焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1169562_comment'></div>圣人之道，以性为中，以情为和，而万物遂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1169562_comment'></div>故人和则气和，气和则天施而生，地顺而成，皆不失其位矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1169562_comment'></div>天地且位，而况于万物乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_127_1169562'>仲尼曰：「君子中庸，小人反中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1169562_comment'></div>君子之中庸也，君子而时中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1169562_comment'></div>小人之中庸也，小人而无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_129_1169562", 1169562, "Clauses/376/Comments/1")'>忌惮</span>也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_130_1169562'>人性莫不善，故君子小人皆有中庸之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1169562_comment'></div>孟子谓恻隐、羞恶、恭逊、是非之心人皆有之是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1169562_comment'></div>惟君子为能明性之善，闲邪窒欲，择乎中庸而守之，故曰：「君子中庸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1169562_comment'></div>小人性以情迁，动而违道，徇乎邪欲，是以「反中庸」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1169562_comment'></div>君子之中庸，所以能守之者，以其道为君子知中庸之不可离，离之非道，故庸言庸行，时不失其中焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1169562_comment'></div>小人之中庸，无以异乎君子之中庸，所以反之而不行者，以其道为小人蔽于情欲之自私，而不知戒忌畏难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_136_1169562'>子曰：「中庸其至矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1169562_comment'></div>民鲜能久矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1169562'>中庸之性，至虚以为体，至神以为用，操之则存，舍之则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1169562_comment'></div>能操而常存则诚，诚则明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1169562_comment'></div>明则能智矣，诚则能圣矣，能圣能智，则可以尽人物之性，成天下之盛德大业，而与天地为一，其德可谓至极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1169562_comment'></div>以其德之至极，故中人已下，其性虽有而不能久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1169562_comment'></div>然则众人之所不能久者，情伪之相感，穿窬之心害之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1169562_comment'></div>善端不能诚固，利欲诱于外，则穿窬之心作，是以难久行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1169562_comment'></div>孟子曰「物交物，则引之而已」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1169562_comment'></div>人知择乎中庸而固执之，终身由之而不失者，圣人之徒与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1169562_comment'></div>孔子之门人，自颜回而下，日亲炙于圣人之教，犹且日月至焉而已，况其下者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1169562_comment'></div>故曰：「民鲜能久矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1169562_comment'></div>子曰：「道之不行也，我知之矣：知者过之，愚者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1169562_comment'></div>道之不明也，我知之矣：贤者过之，不肖者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1169562_comment'></div>人莫不饮食也，鲜能知味也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_151_1169562'>道者，通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1169562_comment'></div>天下由之，无所不通，故谓之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1169562_comment'></div>中庸者，道之本也，惟圣人能尽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1169562_comment'></div>然天下中人之性为多，圣人不以己之所能，强人之所不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1169562_comment'></div>道已隆，则愚不肖者，有所不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1169562_comment'></div>道已杀，则智与贤者，有所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1169562_comment'></div>故圣人本乎中庸，谨是二者之端，用其中道于民，以为天下之通法，使智与贤者俯而就之而不敢过，下文云「有馀，不敢尽」是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1169562_comment'></div>使愚不肖者跂而及之而无不及，下文云「有所不足，不敢不勉」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1169562_comment'></div>如此，然后道可以行，可以明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1169562_comment'></div>孔子谓道之不行也，我知其然矣：夫智者谓其明足以知圣人，而无所不尽，故过之，过之则难继矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1169562_comment'></div>愚者不足以有明也，故不及，不及则有所不勉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1169562_comment'></div>此道之所以不行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1169562_comment'></div>道之不明也，我知其然矣：夫贤者谓其行足以至圣人，而无所不尽，故过之，过则难继矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1169562_comment'></div>不肖者不足与有行也，故不及，不及则有所不勉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1169562_comment'></div>此道之所以不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1169562_comment'></div>道之不行以愚智云者，言乎性之不能明，是以不行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1169562_comment'></div>道之不明以贤不肖云者，言乎行之不能择，是以不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1169562_comment'></div>又以人鲜知道，喻饮食之鲜能知味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1169562_comment'></div>夫五常之于心，人莫不同有也，然而天下之心，独以知道期于圣人者，是知道者寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1169562_comment'></div>五味之于口，人莫不同嗜也，然而天下之口，独以知味期于易牙者，是知味者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1169562_comment'></div>孟子曰：「易牙先得我口之所同嗜者也」，「圣人先得我心之所同然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1169562_comment'></div>故理义之悦我心，犹刍豢之悦我口」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1169562_comment'></div>此以饮食喻道，同斯义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_174_1169562'>子曰：「道其不行矣夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1169562_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_175_1169562'>道之不行有三：过与不及，言乎其才，一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1169562_comment'></div>或出或入，非圣人之正，言乎其术，二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1169562_comment'></div>有其德而无其位，有其位而无其教，言乎其时，三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1169562_comment'></div>孔子之才与术，尽乎群圣人之道，当周之衰，历聘列国，上无明天子，下无贤诸侯能尊用之，因而叹曰：「河不出图，洛不出书，吾已矣夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1169562_comment'></div>盖伤圣人之不作，天下无复知宗予者，故曰：「吾道穷矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1169562_comment'></div>此云道之不行，意在是与！</div><div id='poem_sentence_180_1169562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　陈襄撰《殿中御史陈公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1169571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殿中御史陈君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169571")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169571'>嘉祐六年九月十五日，殿中侍御史里行陈君卒，京师士大夫与之游者吊而哭之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169571_comment'></div>御史中丞等上言乞优加赙赠，与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169571_comment'></div>天子闻而悼之，赐赙钱一十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169571_comment'></div>其弟太子中舍泾与诸孤泣而请铭于君友人陈襄，以志其葬云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169571_comment'></div>君讳洙，字师道，建州建阳人，赠刑部侍郎商之长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169571_comment'></div>少以父荫推与诸弟，力学自奋，以文行称于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169571_comment'></div>举进士高第，为寿、亳、杭三州节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169571_comment'></div>未赴杭，为河北转运使鱼周询奏署掌真定府书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169571_comment'></div>明镐帅府就辟筦机宜事，俄用参知政事丁度荐，召充国子监直讲，改著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169571_comment'></div>大飨明堂，覃恩加秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169571_comment'></div>以侍郎告老还乡，解职太学，治福州之长溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169571_comment'></div>转运使奏监建州茶，未至，丁侍郎忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169571_comment'></div>服除，知湖州之乌程，转太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169571_comment'></div>发运使荐监泗州之转般仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169571_comment'></div>会朝廷建局，编定馆阁所藏书，召入，隶昭文馆编校书籍，迁屯田员外郎，未几擢为御史里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169571_comment'></div>其在寿阳也，与侍中张耆辩事固争，耆虽怒厉声，不为之屈，必直而后止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169571_comment'></div>居亳佐夏英公，有大胥倚势为威福，僚佐无敢指议者，君独发其奸赃，以法黥窜，州人安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169571_comment'></div>明镐辟机宜，军府之政无巨细，一以咨君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169571_comment'></div>乃白简练乡兵以备警急，时号精锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169571_comment'></div>镐还朝及预大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169571_comment'></div>凡两对上前，荐君器业非臣所及，宜居馆阁，其器重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169571_comment'></div>长溪濒海，无耕桑之饶，民鬻盐以为生，禁虽严而盗贩日益众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169571_comment'></div>君至，一切不问，使民衣食，然后修其政刑，道之以礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169571_comment'></div>居二年，狱讼衰息，至有暴悍化为愿民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169571_comment'></div>其治乌程，大概亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169571_comment'></div>君尝病近年台谏之臣言事苛细，不务大体，既居言路，上疏首陈取士、任官、考课之失，乃言馀事，皆有益于国家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169571_comment'></div>一日谓其亲友曰：「吾为御史，得论天下得失，前日之所陈，终非吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169571_comment'></div>方今皇嗣未育，宗庙社稷之计莫大于是，而近臣无敢议者，吾复畏避而无所开陈，则是茍禄自私以欺君父，焉用御史为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169571_comment'></div>吾将言之，万一若不察，继之死而后已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169571_comment'></div>君之将亡也，其日夙兴斋戒言事，疏入未报，而以疾暴卒，人莫知其所言何事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169571_comment'></div>君为人刚正洁直，义形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169571_comment'></div>执亲之丧以孝闻，自敛及葬不为佛事，而一践先王之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169571_comment'></div>居家岂弟，而厚于宗族，与朋友信，闻人之善如己出，虽古人之风节无以尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169571_comment'></div>为政严明，吏不敢欺，至于民事，则多所简恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169571_comment'></div>博涉经史，尤深于《春秋》，为文辞诣理，不事雕饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169571_comment'></div>善品藻人物臧否，有进贤退不肖、澄清中外之志，惜其中道而殒命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169571_comment'></div>尝著《春秋索隐论》五卷，辨诸儒异同之说，盛行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169571_comment'></div>有文数百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169571_comment'></div>享年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169571_comment'></div>曾大父仁鲁为大理评事，大父应期赠官至刑部尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169571_comment'></div>君娶王氏贤淑，生三男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169571_comment'></div>长曰师韩，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169571_comment'></div>次曰师雄、师<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙，）</span>皆幼而好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169571_comment'></div>一女适扬州司法上官垲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169571_comment'></div>卜嘉祐七年月日，葬于建阳考亭乡聚星里之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169571_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1169571'>义充诸中言无邪，忧嗣欲陈乂王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169571_comment'></div>志不克施岂命耶，以铭志之示幽遐。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1169571'></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1169571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年冬</a>　冬，陈襄迁尚书祠部员外郎，出知常州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6eb573ddb304b5baa26298529d09806_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6eb573ddb304b5baa26298529d09806");'><span id='a6eb573ddb304b5baa26298529d09806_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1067')">1063-1067年</a>，47-51岁</div><div id='a6eb573ddb304b5baa26298529d09806' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　由尚书度支员外郎迁尚书司封员外郎，赐五品服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　陈襄召为开封府推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　陈襄在开封府推官任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　陈襄除三司监铁判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　陈襄作《苏明允府君判词》<div id='poem_163524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏明允府君挽词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163524")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163524'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163524'>礼阁仪新奏，延英席久虚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163524'>自从掩关卧，无复草玄书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163524'>东府先生诔，西山孝子庐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163524'>谁言身后事，文止似相如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163524'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163524_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄作《奉使回上殿札子》<div id='poem_1169410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>治平四年八月奉使回上殿劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169410")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169410'>臣昨奉使北蕃，久留边郡，窃见高阳关一路沿边州郡戍兵甚冗，马步之卒，不减三万九千馀人，岁费刍粮，动以万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169410_comment'></div>诸州储偫之数，出于贵籴，多者无数岁之备，少者微三年之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169410_comment'></div>一甲未擐，则财用已匮，而边民困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169410_comment'></div>幸而亭障无虞，可以姑息，一有警急，如何支持？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169410_comment'></div>臣愚以为方今安边息民之要，莫先于减戍卒而用土兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169410_comment'></div>戍卒减则财用省而民力纾，土兵用则战守易而城池固，此祖宗御戎之遗策，不可废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169410_comment'></div>今延安本路七州四军义勇之籍，无虑四万六千馀人，可以当马步戍兵之数，但官司因循，失于训练，岁时虽有教阅之名，而无可用之实，甚可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169410_comment'></div>况边防诸郡，深池高垒，有陂塘沮洳之阻，无犬羊奔冲之患，万一有寇至，不过坚吾壁以守之，清吾野以待之，则昔时义勇之军，足为防捍之用，不有屯戍，又何患哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169410_comment'></div>臣欲请朝廷先遣才望之臣，按行一路，令与监司长吏将所籍义勇人数重行检点，去其老弱，而补之壮勇，舍其征役，而授以骑耕，每于农隙之时，给与口食，选差教队，使臣分往诸邑，精加简阅，务令精锐，可以效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169410_comment'></div>然后减去戍兵之半，食于近辅之郡，遇大征伐，则发内卒以应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169410_comment'></div>如此则土有精兵，塞有馀粟，守御有备，而边民苏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169410_comment'></div>如允所奏，乞降付枢密院相度施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169410_comment'></div>今取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄迁工部郎中，充秘阁校理，出知明州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄作《英宗皇帝挽词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在本年，地点疑在京城。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄撰《左侍禁陆公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在本年，地点疑在京城。）</span><div id='poem_1169569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左侍禁陆君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169569")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169569'>君讳廙，字彦恭，故司封员外郎、集贤校理广之同母弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169569_comment'></div>其先吴郡人，四世徙居福州侯官县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169569_comment'></div>曾祖讳景迁，为吴越骁卫上将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169569_comment'></div>祖讳崇扆，以威武军观察推官从钱氏举国归朝，官至殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169569_comment'></div>考讳中和，赠官至职方员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169569_comment'></div>生二子，君其季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169569_comment'></div>君累进士，常与廷试，庆历二年春特奏名，试中方略，为三班奉职，四转至左侍禁，历官河中府及建州、剑州、汀州、邵武军五巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169569_comment'></div>以母太君居京师，就监顺成仓，遂为泉州兵马监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169569_comment'></div>母丧，乞解官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169569_comment'></div>服除，用三司判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169569_comment'></div>今翰林侍读滕公甫奏举监饶州之铸钱监，未行，以疾卒于京师，享年六十有二，即治平二年四月朔旦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169569_comment'></div>为人孝友，少事母兄，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169569_comment'></div>初，职方之亡，母太君以二子幼，不克起家为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169569_comment'></div>校理与君闻之，相与泣涕，发愤就学，置书数千卷，闭门诵之不休，而校理登甲科，君虽连蹇场屋，益自刻苦，以至得官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169569_comment'></div>其后陆氏相继登第者凡数人，闾里称为显族，校理与君之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169569_comment'></div>君姿性沉厚，而色严毅若不可犯，久与之处，温温然若不能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169569_comment'></div>居官小心而谨畏，与人恭而有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169569_comment'></div>娶吴氏贤淑，故太常博士讳千仞之女，生二子，曰宪元，登进士科，卒于开封府祥符县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169569_comment'></div>次曰长宾，蔡州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169569_comment'></div>咸有善行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169569_comment'></div>一女适起居舍人知谏院陈襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169569_comment'></div>孙男六人，恂、悚、忱、恺、恽、恪，尚幼，皆俊敏而好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169569_comment'></div>长宾奉丧归福唐，以治平四年三月己酉葬于州城之东闽县孝义里，以从考妣之墓，成君志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169569_comment'></div>考以校理故赠官，享年五十有六，卒于天禧三年十月六日，葬于五年十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169569_comment'></div>妣林氏，叙封寿安县太君，享年八十有四，卒于嘉祐六年二月二十七日，葬于七年八月初七日，去君之茔盖百步，所谓瑞圣里也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169569_comment'></div>墓皆无志，襄谨铭君之竁，而附卒葬云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169569_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1169569'>行己恭，居官勤，不愧于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169569_comment'></div>生能养，死归葬，不离于亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169569_comment'></div>善有泽，躬不亨，在后人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1169569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄撰《开封府祥符县主簿陆君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在本年，地点疑在京城。）</span><div id='poem_1169570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府祥符县主簿陆君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169570")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169570'>河南陆君，讳宪元，字道祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169570_comment'></div>生而奇俊，其母吴氏贤而常亲教之，曾未数岁，通习群书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169570_comment'></div>十七岁来京师，从聱隅先生黄晞治《易》、《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169570_comment'></div>晞畏其才，不敢以弟子处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169570_comment'></div>其为文章，落笔数千言，辞理典奥难读，有自名一家之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169570_comment'></div>累举进士不第，既而叹曰：「人莫吾知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169570_comment'></div>丈夫不获已而干禄养，乌用犛牛以捕鼠哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169570_comment'></div>自是稍稍习为声律，其辞务于精丽明白，而归之閒暇，学者多宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169570_comment'></div>嘉祐二年赐进士出身，为陈州司户参军，再调开封府祥符县主簿，待次都下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169570_comment'></div>治平元年二月六日遇疾以卒，享年四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169570_comment'></div>缙绅闻人素与之游者，相与哭而敛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169570_comment'></div>君少负奇才，志气豪放，常谓功名可以坐致，而富贵不足用吾力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169570_comment'></div>既应举沮衄，复为小吏奔走，忧愁悔咎，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169570_comment'></div>由此揉练人事，养心治性，泊然有宽厚老成之风，虽临之以得丧荣辱，气无所挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169570_comment'></div>居家恺弟，与朋友信，通财而好施，知以节义自重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169570_comment'></div>论议时事，雅有器识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169570_comment'></div>大臣有欲置之文字职者，遽以不受命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169570_comment'></div>君之先世事吴越，五代祖避唐季之乱，自吴迁闽，遂为侯官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169570_comment'></div>曾大父福州观察推官，讳崇扆，从钱氏纳土始为皇朝官，终于殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169570_comment'></div>至君之伯父司封员外郎集贤校理讳广，而子孙始显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169570_comment'></div>大父以校理故赠职方员外郎，讳中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169570_comment'></div>父故左侍禁，讳廙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169570_comment'></div>妻刘氏，生三男，悚、恽、恪，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169570_comment'></div>弟长宾，奉君之丧以归，卜治平四年三月己酉，葬于福州东门之外闽县孝义里祖考茔之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169570_comment'></div>襄实娶君之女弟，而知其行，谨志其墓，为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1169570'>呜呼君乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169570_comment'></div>才非不足兮，辞固有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169570_comment'></div>习险虑患兮，志气和舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169570_comment'></div>既培且覆兮，命也何如！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1169570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　陈襄作《祭黄虞部文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在本年，地点疑在京城。）</span><div id='poem_1169579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭浦城黄虞部瑊文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169579")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169579'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169579'>某曩为属吏，最荷公知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169579_comment'></div>自闻公丧，攀号无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169579_comment'></div>此者被命，出守四明，归省松楸，道过坟下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169579_comment'></div>追惟恩旧，涕泗横流，薄奠斯陈，以告于幽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1169579_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f42d0aa1555f4d38941974b3e9e4327d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f42d0aa1555f4d38941974b3e9e4327d");'><span id='f42d0aa1555f4d38941974b3e9e4327d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1071')">1069-1071年</a>，53-55岁</div><div id='f42d0aa1555f4d38941974b3e9e4327d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年夏</a>　夏，陈襄到阙，迁尚书刑部郎中，修起居注，知谏院，管勾国子监公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年秋</a>　秋，除侍御史知杂事，有旨候知制诰阙召试。公上疏力解，诏从之。兼判吏部流内铨，赐三品服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年秋</a>　陈襄作《辞修起居注知谏院》四状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《修起居注举自代状》<div id='poem_1169372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修起居注举自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169372")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169372'>臣伏见阙郎中集贤校理冯浩，困不失亨，恬而有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169372_comment'></div>俾居左史之任，宜有近臣之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169372_comment'></div>臣实不如，今举自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169372_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1169372_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《侍御史知杂事举自代状》<div id='poem_1169373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>侍御史知杂事举自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169373")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169373'>臣伏见前授安州司户参军、充国子监直讲陈烈，根明诚之学，躬孝悌之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169373_comment'></div>非圣人之书不读，非先王之法不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169373_comment'></div>穷泰不累于心，出处必由于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169373_comment'></div>使居清宪之地，必有古人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169373_comment'></div>臣实不如，今举自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169373_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1169373_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《辞中书候试知制诰状》<div id='poem_1169374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞中书候试知制诰状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169374")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169374'>臣蒙恩除侍御史知杂事，仍准中书劄子，奉圣旨候知制诰有阙与试，劄付御史台者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169374_comment'></div>臣闻命之次，震惶无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169374_comment'></div>窃惟陛下必以臣自内史过为台杂，乃是下迁，爰降德音，俾谕圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169374_comment'></div>在臣之分，诚所未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169374_comment'></div>陛下以义使臣，臣当惟命是听，岂可计校资地，以为重轻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169374_comment'></div>况知杂之任，号为雄剧，陛下柬求才哲，未尝轻授，而独以臣充选，其责非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169374_comment'></div>故臣之区区，惟惧不职，无以称陛下任使之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169374_comment'></div>谨当夙夜上裨朝政，下正台纲，震肃百僚，纠绳非法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169374_comment'></div>义之所在，知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169374_comment'></div>夫岂知鈇钺之在前，而宠禄之居后哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169374_comment'></div>一有顾利避害之心，则依违姑息，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169374_comment'></div>身且不正，焉能正人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169374_comment'></div>臣虽不然，宁免公议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169374_comment'></div>所有先降中书劄子，候知制诰有阙与试指挥，伏望特行追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169374_comment'></div>候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1169374'>〔附录〕右奉圣旨：依奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169374_comment'></div>所有元降劄子，宜令御史台缴纳中书省。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1169374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《赴召修注上殿劄子》<div id='poem_1169385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴召修注上殿劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169385")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169385'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169385'>臣闻为人君者在知至道，其次务得贤，其次务修法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169385_comment'></div>知斯三者，则知所以治天下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169385_comment'></div>至道之要，求之不远，在乎养心治性，择乎中庸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169385_comment'></div>天之所命之谓性，性之未变之谓中，中者天下之大本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169385_comment'></div>而有五善，其端也，若甚微而不可明，及其至也，塞乎天地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169385_comment'></div>感物而动之谓情，情者天下之大欲也，而有邪有正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169385_comment'></div>率善而行之谓正，率不善而行之谓邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169385_comment'></div>故正者天之道也，邪者人之伪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169385_comment'></div>苟得其正，则彼之所谓情者，喜也，怒也，哀也，乐也，无所处而不为中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169385_comment'></div>即《易》之《乾》曰：「利贞者，性情是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169385_comment'></div>苟失之邪，则吾之所谓善者，仁也，义也，礼也，智也，信也，无所往而不为伪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169385_comment'></div>即孟轲所谓「物交物，则引之而已」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169385_comment'></div>尧舜得之天，故曰「性之也」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169385_comment'></div>禹汤治之人，故曰「身之也」，正矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169385_comment'></div>五霸失之伪，故曰「假之也」，邪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169385_comment'></div>是王霸之辨，而君子之所以慎择者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169385_comment'></div>其始也，在于博学以尽其心，尽心以明其善，明善以持其志，持志以养其气，养气以充其体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169385_comment'></div>诚至于高明博厚而不息也，然后能定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169385_comment'></div>明至于广大精微而不惑也，然后能应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169385_comment'></div>能定能应，则七情者不能伪，而五事者无所不至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169385_comment'></div>喜非吾喜也，而未尝不喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169385_comment'></div>怒非吾怒也，而未尝不怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169385_comment'></div>哀乐非吾哀乐也，而未尝无哀乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169385_comment'></div>莫不与天下公共之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169385_comment'></div>其为貌也，必正礼而无所不庄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169385_comment'></div>其为言也，必正辞而无所不治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169385_comment'></div>其为视也，必正色而无所不辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169385_comment'></div>其为听也，必正音而无所不谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169385_comment'></div>其为思也，必正道而无所不达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169385_comment'></div>故其应务也，举天下之变，不得以困其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169385_comment'></div>其任人也，举天下之才，不得以罔吾道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169385_comment'></div>其治民也，举天下之政，不得以盭吾仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169385_comment'></div>其行法也，举天下之情，不得以易吾义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169385_comment'></div>迩之则虚一而静，远之则通乎伦类而知，建诸天地而不悖，质诸鬼神而无疑，百世以俟圣人而不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169385_comment'></div>斯道也，百王之所相传而不易者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169385_comment'></div>君得之传之臣，臣得之致之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169385_comment'></div>大者以为圣，小者以为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169385_comment'></div>或并世而其身传，或异世而其言示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169385_comment'></div>尧之于舜、禹、皋陶，则以身传之也，彼则见而知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169385_comment'></div>于汤、文王，则以言示之也，彼则闻而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169385_comment'></div>文王之于武王、周公、太公，则以身传之也，彼则见而知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169385_comment'></div>于孔子、孟轲，则以言而示之也，彼则闻而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169385_comment'></div>伊尹之于太甲也，甘盘之于高宗也，周公之于成王也，尝致之矣，而天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169385_comment'></div>孔子、孟轲不得其君而致之也，而天下乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169385_comment'></div>行乎百世之上，言乎百世之下，而若合符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169385_comment'></div>其用舍则殊，其所以传之者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169385_comment'></div>为人君者，有其道，则聪明不足以自任也，可以取而取之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169385_comment'></div>有其位，则权势不足以自私也，可以与而与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169385_comment'></div>故其心公焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169385_comment'></div>居天下之广居，揽天下之多务，而不敢独为之也，必求天下之贤者而任之，相与共济焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169385_comment'></div>尧非不圣也，方其洪水之时，中国犹未乂，尧思天下之贤者宜莫如舜，举而敷治焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169385_comment'></div>舜思天下之贤者宜莫如禹，又以命禹洎诸臣，水土既平，益火山泽，禽兽之害人者去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169385_comment'></div>稷教耕稼，民得安居而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169385_comment'></div>又惧夫无教而乱也，使契为司徒，教以人伦，而皋陶以刑辅之，而天下以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169385_comment'></div>故孔子曰：「舜有臣五人而天下治」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169385_comment'></div>孟轲曰：「尧以不得舜为己忧，舜以不得禹、皋陶为己忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169385_comment'></div>知其所以为大也，得其小者以失其大者，乌足以为尧舜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169385_comment'></div>隋文帝每一临朝，或至日昃，宿卫之士传餐而食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169385_comment'></div>唐文宗议政延英，每对宰臣，率漏下十数刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169385_comment'></div>此二主者，非不用心勤劳，然终无益于治者，由亲细务而闇大体，不知其术然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169385_comment'></div>皋陶曰：「元首丛脞哉，股肱惰哉，万事隳哉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1169385_comment'></div>此可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1169385_comment'></div>夫法度者，人情之防范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1169385_comment'></div>为国而不修先王之法度，是犹输之不以规矩正方圆，旷之不以六律治五音也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1169385_comment'></div>古者，先王建国，一事一政，无非法者，将以定民之志，而立民之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1169385_comment'></div>虽其迹之不必同，然其制作之意，不可一日而忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1169385_comment'></div>故其车服宫室皆有度数，人徒械用皆有等宜，贡赋必有节，师田学射皆有法，冠昏丧祭皆有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1169385_comment'></div>奸声奸色者举废，乱名乱政者举杀，器服不中度者举毁，禽兽不中杀者举禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1169385_comment'></div>是以国家优裕，风俗淳一，而物无疵疠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1169385_comment'></div>周衰，礼乐坏，王道陵夷，上无圣贤之君，下无法度之臣，天下荡然无纲纪制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1169385_comment'></div>汉兴，有仲舒者，可谓法度之臣矣，而无可致之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1169385_comment'></div>唐太宗有为之主也，而房、杜之徒，不足以言礼乐，此其所以不王也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1169385_comment'></div>伏惟陛下享国以来，孜孜庶政，二帝三王之事，必欲举而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1169385_comment'></div>臣居斯时，不以尧舜之道陈于陛下之前，则不恭之罪莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1169385_comment'></div>昔者孟轲见滕文公，言必称尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1169385_comment'></div>文公，中才之主也，轲犹以此待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1169385_comment'></div>况陛下天资圣德、聪明智勇之若此，臣敢隐默而不言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1169385_comment'></div>方今天下之患者，皆谓黎民未乂，戎狄未恭，政令未明，财用不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1169385_comment'></div>以臣思之，不足为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1169385_comment'></div>所以过虑者，在陛下中庸之未择，性理之未充，贤才之未多，法度之未立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1169385_comment'></div>伏望陛下略机务之繁，进诚明之学，稽经信道，颐养神明，慎选缙绅有道之臣，旁求岩穴笃行之士，日与讲求性命之理、道德之源，养而充之，以至神固，斯可以不言而化矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1169385_comment'></div>然后建学校，隆师儒，首自京师，达于州邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1169385_comment'></div>群百辟之才以长育之，隆三物之教以统一之，则贤人众多，足以任使矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1169385_comment'></div>求一德以居论道之司，择庶尹以付任官之责，间用儒臣以分按察之权，均布循吏以膺守宰之寄，自然百司群吏莫不任职，政令自均而黎元安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1169385_comment'></div>诏奉常，以礼学之士修五礼于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1169385_comment'></div>委大农，以制置之司节百用于国，则浮费自省，而财用有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1169385_comment'></div>陛下身先恭俭，以训于上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1169385_comment'></div>小大之臣，畏法遵绳，以守于下，民以是化，政以是淳，国富兵强，可以制挺以挞戎狄之兵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1169385_comment'></div>凡有司之事，一切付之，陛下但优游岩廊，以神道设教，此尧舜之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1169385_comment'></div>《易》曰：「火在天上，大有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1169385_comment'></div>君子以遏恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1169385", 1169385, "Clauses/300/Comments/0")'>扬善</span>，顺天休命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1169385_comment'></div>惟陛下不以臣言为迂阔，少赐留意，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1169385_comment'></div>取进止<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1169385_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1169385'>彼：原无，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_93_1169385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169385'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1169385_0'>⑴ 《古灵先生文集》卷一五。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷二，《历代名臣奏议》卷三五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169385_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《进诚明说并劄子》<div id='poem_1169386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进诚明说劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169386")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169386'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169386'>臣学术荒疏，行能无取，先朝备位馆阁，无补朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169386_comment'></div>臣非偷禄养安之人，惟以位卑言轻，未为朝廷所信重，以时流奔竞好进，臣实耻之，是以居常退缩，以道自守，人亦无知臣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169386_comment'></div>不谓陛下过采虚名，特于流辈之中不次进用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169386_comment'></div>臣自度不肖，再三辞避，不蒙圣恩俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169386_comment'></div>夙夜忧惧，难胜其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169386_comment'></div>然臣虽愚无他长，惟少嗜圣人经籍之学，自谓得其门户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169386_comment'></div>及观诸子百氏书，质正是非，然后益知臣之所学，不少盭于尧、舜、文、武、孔、孟之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169386_comment'></div>伏睹陛下天资圣性，聪明颖悟，而又好学，求治之心如此之至，臣敢不竭愚自效，日以此道布陈于陛下之前？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169386_comment'></div>臣又仰思陛下今日所先之务，无大于明诚之学，德成道充，然后可以临照天下，裁成万务，而归之皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169386_comment'></div>臣谨先撰成《诚明之说》一篇，大约以子思、孟轲之学为主，而取其精要，随而解释，庶几至道之奥，昭然可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169386_comment'></div>谨具投进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169386_comment'></div>伏望陛下不以臣言为迂诞，留神采纳，非独臣之幸也，天下之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169386_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《知谏院进劄子》<div id='poem_1169420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知谏院进劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169420")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169420'>臣闻君之视臣，犹心膂之于股肱、耳目也，四者相资而成一体，则不劳而功用成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169420_comment'></div>故公卿者，人君之股肱，而台谏为其耳目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169420_comment'></div>故古之人君用谏诤之臣，必求方直辨博之士，司其视听而补其阙遗，其心鳃鳃然恐不闻切直之言，以救其失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169420_comment'></div>故舜戒其臣曰「臣作朕股肱、耳目」，又曰「予违汝弼，汝无面从，退有后言」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169420_comment'></div>古之人臣谏诤其君，苟可以言，虽鈇锧之在前，无所忌讳者，欲以致君之无过，而非所以暴其恶，将以效臣之节，而非取其名，盖居言责之任，其义当尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169420_comment'></div>故《易》曰「王臣蹇蹇，匪躬之故」，《书》曰「斯谋斯猷，惟我后之德」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169420_comment'></div>故君臣之际，同心协德，义成一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169420_comment'></div>上之人茍闻一言之善，则雍容听纳，不以为暴已而无所疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169420_comment'></div>下之人茍闻一事之失，则周旋切争，不以为干誉而无所惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169420_comment'></div>此所谓信而后谏者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169420_comment'></div>伏望圣慈少察臣之言，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169420_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1169420_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《乞正台谏官劄子》<div id='poem_1169421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞正台谏官劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169421")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169421'>臣窃以谏臣司衮职之阙，格君心之非，台官纠正朝纲，绳百官之失，明其职之各异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169421_comment'></div>伏睹近年台官侵谏诤之职，谏臣言风宪之事，此孔子所谓名不正而言不顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169421_comment'></div>臣今欲乞谏臣惟司人君言动之过，补时政阙失之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169421_comment'></div>若夫百僚之愆缪，台纲之不振，则有御史在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169421_comment'></div>庶几台谏之任，皆得专职，而言责不紊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169421_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1169421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《议学校贡举劄子》<div id='poem_1169427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议学校贡举劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169427")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169427'>臣伏睹先降诏书，令两制已下至台阁臣僚建议学校贡举之制，得以上闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169427_comment'></div>兹见陛下讲求至治，思得求贤养士之要，以兴起王业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169427_comment'></div>臣近以谏官兼领国子监事，每至太学，视其斋舍颓敝，生徒佻达，官吏苟简，殊无法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169427_comment'></div>窃谓太学者，天子教化之宫，自古圣帝贤王，莫之敢废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169427_comment'></div>晋汉而下，虽无先王之法，然犹置师弟子多至千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169427_comment'></div>唐贞观中，规制益广，增筑学舍千二百间，博士生员与藩夷子弟游于学者，仅至八千馀员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169427_comment'></div>岂国朝儒学之盛跨越汉唐，而弦诵之地寂寥至此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169427_comment'></div>臣实耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169427_comment'></div>盖艺祖创制，未遑斯事，当时谋议之臣，识虑不远，因循百年，未有太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169427_comment'></div>今生员所居，乃是司业厅事，与朝集数位而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169427_comment'></div>天下徯望，必行于陛下之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169427_comment'></div>事得其本，为之甚易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169427_comment'></div>但陛下先求贤哲之士，使居师长之位，百度兴葺，乃其末事，可以不劳而成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169427_comment'></div>伏见前授试大理评事、充忠武军节度推官、知许州长社县事常秩，性行纯明，专于古学，甘贫守道，不茍仕进，语默出处，非义不由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169427_comment'></div>道德未加而人信之，此可谓以身治人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169427_comment'></div>前授安州司户参军、充国子监直讲陈烈，忠孝仁勇，根于诚性，行与道合，心与俗违，博通群经，而尤明于礼学，思一物不获其所，则其心忧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169427_comment'></div>仁宗朝尝以学官召之，数命不起，此可谓能自任以天下之重者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169427_comment'></div>二子之道则同，而其用或异，皆所谓学孔子者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169427_comment'></div>方今丘园有道之士，求烈与秩，未见其比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169427_comment'></div>陛下方大有为之时，舍如是人，而使穷居家食，恐非虞舜之举十六相、文王待二老之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169427_comment'></div>如陛下未即置诸左右，姑以礼命召至太学，使居博士之职，以经授弟子，帅公室公卿之子弟与国之俊选，咸得执经肄业，而以师礼处之，庶乎其可致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169427_comment'></div>有乡贡进士管师常者，履行正固，经术专精，东南士人，多所从学，更练民事，而适于时用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169427_comment'></div>尝为太学正，众论推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169427_comment'></div>乡贡进士程颐者，有高坚之行，怀经济之学，廷试不第，无复进取，守道用晦，名闻公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169427_comment'></div>近闻诸路搜访遗逸以应赦书，师常与颐，咸与荐达，亦望圣恩并除国子监一助教之名，庶几太学生员有所规法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169427_comment'></div>《语》曰：「举逸民，天下之民归心焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169427_comment'></div>正谓此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169427_comment'></div>所有近诏诸臣议学之制，论者固多，伏望陛下选择近臣，颁付详定，取其合于王制者，立为一代之法，固不为浅者之论而遂沮止，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169427_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1169427_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《乞免御史刘述等罪状》<div id='poem_1169388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免御史刘述等言事罪状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169388")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169388'>臣近者窃闻侍御史知杂事刘述以缴敕被劾，前日御史刘琦、钱顗又以言事责降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169388_comment'></div>寻准同知谏院范纯仁牒，称为台官刘琦等责降，有状奏乞留逐官，及言参知政事王安石事，居家待罪，更不供职，乞行贬窜，牒院照会者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169388_comment'></div>臣亦备位谏官，端视朝廷上下之情乖戾若此，臣实忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169388_comment'></div>陛下始者知安石之贤，擢与大政，天下闻之，莫不相贺，以为陛下有知人之哲，能任道德之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169388_comment'></div>陛下责望安石之意既深，则安石论报陛下之心愈急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169388_comment'></div>事既伤于欲速，人不免乎有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169388_comment'></div>台谏耳目之官，茍有见闻，不敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169388_comment'></div>事之可否，在陛下择而行之，不宜小有忤旨，便加谴斥，恐非所以通下情、来谏诤之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169388_comment'></div>自陛下享国以来，凡五易御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169388_comment'></div>台谏之官，罢斥相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169388_comment'></div>以不失职而去，固无所损，然而天下之人皆谓陛下不能包容听纳，窒塞贤路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169388_comment'></div>「訑訑之声音颜色，拒人于千里之外」，在于圣政，不为无损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169388_comment'></div>况今官政因循，上下无守，述为刑曹，缴敕待罪，可谓不失其职矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169388_comment'></div>若陛下因此罪之，是使天下偷禄茍安之人，益隳官守矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169388_comment'></div>况御史之任，得以纠正朝纲，今琦与顗为言执政之臣，虽风闻失实，未为深过，若以微罪被逐，是使言事之官，无复敢论柄臣之阙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169388_comment'></div>此窃为陛下惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169388_comment'></div>夫天地之所以为大者，以其善覆万物而不可名，善载万物而不可度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169388_comment'></div>圣人之德，亦在容之而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169388_comment'></div>《书》曰：「必有忍，其乃有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169388_comment'></div>有容，德乃大」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169388_comment'></div>愿陛下不以守职违诏，而置述于法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169388_comment'></div>不以言诋近臣，而重琦等之罪，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169388_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1169388_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《论制置三司条列乞行均输法状》<div id='poem_1169425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论三司条例乞行均输法劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169425")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169425'>臣伏睹中书劄子、制置三司条例司状奏，乞行均输之法，朝廷遂除司勋郎中薛向充江淮制置发运使，以领其事，又出内帑之钱数百万贯，使之笼货取息，以助县官之经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169425_comment'></div>臣窃以为兴利之道，非当今之所宜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169425_comment'></div>陛下圣德文明，超越前古，即位之初，天下皆谓二帝三王之政必行于今日，岂宜先利以示四方？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169425_comment'></div>臣为谏官，姑息而不言，致陛下于有过之地，是不以尧舜之道期于陛下，臣实耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169425_comment'></div>自先皇顾命已来，当国家多难之际，天文谪见于上，地道震动于下，水潦民饥之灾遍于中国，此天意有以警动陛下，欲其恐惧修德，而保其全安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169425_comment'></div>而陛下首当修明五事，钦慎万几，务一德以享天心，思一言以和天下，曾未及此，乃欲徇有司之议，行桑弘羊榷利之术，臣不知其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169425_comment'></div>昔汉武帝承文、景恭俭之后，国用富饶，侈心一生，遂有轻事四夷之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169425_comment'></div>中道劳费，帑庾空竭，乃以弘羊为大司农中丞，置均输平准之法，笼天下之货物，买贱卖贵，以资一时之急，卒敛怨于天下，贻讥于后世，是岂仁术哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169425_comment'></div>陛下若以国用空虚，调度滋广，不榷利无以继公上之给，臣窃以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169425_comment'></div>陛下尊为天子，富有方夏，四海九州之赋入，不为不多，第以承平百年，因循奢靡，而制用无节，此今日不足之患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169425_comment'></div>近者，朝廷深鉴其失，亲命近臣辟选官属，制置三司条例固已救其深弊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169425_comment'></div>但令所司取天下会计之籍，度县官供给之数，百度为之均节，而归之艺极，至于无名之费，不急之务，一切禁之而不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169425_comment'></div>诸路财赋之有无，令有司得以便宜移用，与凡籴买上供之物，皆得以徙贵就贱，用近易远，使无害于公私，而止于备用可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169425_comment'></div>而后陛下身先恭俭，节用爱人而率之于上，小大之臣畏法遵绳而守之于下，如此则浮费自省，而财物不可胜用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169425_comment'></div>又何必收轻重敛散归之公上，与民争锥刀之利，而失王政之体乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169425_comment'></div>孟子对梁惠王曰：「王何必曰利，亦有仁义而已矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169425_comment'></div>「未有仁而遗其亲，未有义而后其君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169425_comment'></div>子贡曰：「文武之道未坠于地，在人，贤者识其大者，不贤者识其小者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169425_comment'></div>夫道，亦在择之而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169425_comment'></div>所有贷钱贾贩之事，如以臣言为可采，特赐寝而不行，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169425_comment'></div>取进止<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169425_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1169425'>「即位」前原有「作其」二字，据库本删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1169425_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169425'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1169425_0'>⑴ 《古灵先生文集》卷一八。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一○九，《历代名臣奏议》卷二六六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169425_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《弹刘攽王介状》<div id='poem_1169409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹刘攽王介状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169409")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169409'>臣窃以刘攽、王介，在试院忿争，为台官张瑨等弹奏，已奉圣旨，免勘赎金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169409_comment'></div>朝廷虽示宽恩，物议未以为允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169409_comment'></div>攽、介皆以文学被选，置之馆阁，不思修蕴器业，以为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169409_comment'></div>攽惟尚气淩人，动为嘲侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169409_comment'></div>介特褊心好竞，所至喧悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169409_comment'></div>率行若此，人何以观？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169409_comment'></div>增长浇浮，损坏风教，无甚于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169409_comment'></div>欲乞深示戒惩，特行贬斥，俾居于外，改过自新，不惟攽、介之福，抑朝廷忠厚之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169409_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1169409_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《论祖无择下狱状》<div id='poem_1169398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论祖无择下狱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169398")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169398'>臣昨蒙恩召赴阙，道由杭州，伏见知州龙图阁学士祖无择为政宽平，爱民无扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169398_comment'></div>杭为剧府，素号难治，前后守臣多以暴刻绳民，故无择之治，百姓安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169398_comment'></div>近者，只因监察御史里行王子韶察访过实，遂兴大狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169398_comment'></div>自无择下吏，州人皇皇如系父母，斋僧祈福，为之涕雪于府，以至诣阙告诉，非无择惠政，得民之深，何以至此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169398_comment'></div>访闻勘官惨礉，百端锻鍊，天子近臣既为狱吏耻辱，刻木画地，莫不招承，窃虑讯鞫之间未免冤滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169398_comment'></div>臣始闻诏狱，恐无择别有赃污之状，故不敢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169398_comment'></div>近得所知殿中丞知湖州归安县柯述书，具言其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169398_comment'></div>述是前来勘官，宜得事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169398_comment'></div>伏望圣慈以无择尝为侍臣，秉心忠实，但以宽而泛爱，失于周防，狱案未成，特赐驰驿指挥，早令结绝，使无择出外听敕，如别无踰违大恶，即乞贷从宽典，不惟无伤堂陛之体，亦足以慰士民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169398_comment'></div>所有柯述书，谨随状缴进以闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1169398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈襄作《乞疏放秀越二狱干系人状》<div id='poem_1169397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞疏放秀越二狱干系人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169397")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169397'>臣伏见中书劄子，差屯田郎中沈衡、著作佐郎张载，往秀、越二州，置司推勘祖无择、苗振公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169397_comment'></div>风闻其间因缘作过及干连照證人数不少，若依制勘条例，并须逐一勾追證对圆结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169397_comment'></div>缘杭、明二州去勘所各经数舍，往来追摄，不无骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169397_comment'></div>窃以朝廷诏狱，本为守臣违越，为害于民，以此差官取勘，若令无辜干系之人，一例拘留对辨，或因累被罪，反为平人之害，甚非陛下绳吏爱民之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169397_comment'></div>欲乞特降指挥，下逐处勘官，只令取勘祖无择、苗振及见禁作过情理切害之人所犯重罪，依例追呼照證结绝，以申惩诫外，其馀罪轻不坐，与应系干證之人，如已勾追，即立时取状疏放，其未勾追者，并免追究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169397_comment'></div>及虽有小可罪愆，本州作过因被连累之人，亦乞出自圣慈，特与推恩矜放，更不具案圆结施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169397_comment'></div>所贵不至滋蔓淹延，别致骚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169397_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1169397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年春</a>　春，陈襄召试知制诰。公自言尝论常平新法，不听，辞不就试。执政以为当出，乃欲罢御史，以集贤殿修撰、陕西转运使。敕未下，上批别进呈，谓执政曰：“吴申全不能讲，欲候陈某受职，留讲筵。”于是除秘阁校理，复修起居注，直舍人院，兼天章阁侍讲，仍判铨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《辞中书召试知制诰状》<div id='poem_1169375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞中书召试知制诰状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169375")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169375'>某今月二十一日准中书召臣言，有圣旨令就试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169375_comment'></div>闻命之次，震悚不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169375_comment'></div>臣学术至疏，昨得误蒙陛下擢寘谏垣，曾未踰时，就迁台杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169375_comment'></div>仍准中书劄子，奉圣旨候知制诰有阙与试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169375_comment'></div>臣以风宪之任，言责非轻，岂宜首戴法冠，而心怀宠利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169375_comment'></div>寻陈封奏，乞追还原降劄子指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169375_comment'></div>陛下深察其心，特蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169375_comment'></div>备员几岁，无补朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169375_comment'></div>比以制置条例一司，改更朝廷新法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169375_comment'></div>中外之议，皆以为扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169375_comment'></div>臣负忧责，不得不言，未能开悟圣心，早令寝罢，是臣不职之罪，未知谴所，岂可辄为私计，进冒宠荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169375_comment'></div>况今青苗之法尚行，而言事者继去，抨弹之际，正在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169375_comment'></div>惟陛下用臣之言，则臣虽窃位宪司，且愿供职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169375_comment'></div>如其不用，则日俟窜斥，岂有荣进之望哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169375_comment'></div>所有召试指挥，臣不敢当，伏乞特赐追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169375_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169375_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《申中书省状》<div id='poem_1169376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞召试知制诰申中书省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169376")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169376'>某今月二十一日准中书召某言，有圣旨令某试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169376_comment'></div>某以学术至疏，言事不职，岂敢辄为私计，进冒宠荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169376_comment'></div>所有召试指挥，伏乞赐追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169376_comment'></div>除已具状敷奏外，谨具状申中书省，伏候裁旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1169376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《辞直舍人院判吏部流内铨敕内名衔状》<div id='poem_1169380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞直舍人院兼判吏部流内铨兼天章阁侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169380")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169380'>臣近尝有状敷奏，辞免直舍人院及兼判吏部流内铨兼天章阁侍讲恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169380_comment'></div>今月十二日，准中书劄子，奉圣旨不许辞免，仰便受敕牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169380_comment'></div>今月十三日，延和殿侍立，又蒙内臣传宣，召臣面谕圣旨，令臣受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169380_comment'></div>臣虽再三辞避，不蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169380_comment'></div>又以侍讲之命，前来已降，御批宣谕，责臣以经义之益，亦令勿辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169380_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，上荷圣恩之厚，皇恐之际，难以固违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169380_comment'></div>退而思之，终是义理未安，不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169380_comment'></div>故臣区区之诚，尚有未尽者，不避罪戮，须至再烦天听，惟陛下俯加察允，则愚臣幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169380_comment'></div>臣闻之，君子之仕，行其义也，非以为利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169380_comment'></div>夫所谓义者，食其食而忧其事，不以一身之所利，而忘天下之所患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169380_comment'></div>道之行也，言之从也，虽禄之以万钟而不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169380_comment'></div>道之不行也，言之不从也，则致为臣而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169380_comment'></div>此古人之所以去就也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169380_comment'></div>今也中国一君，内外莫非其臣，舍乎是，则夷狄之国，无可去之义矣。<div class='inline'
