id='poem_sentence_13_1169380_comment'></div>故其道之不行，言之不用，乌乎之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169380_comment'></div>必也辞尊以居卑，辞富以居贫，辞内以居外，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169380_comment'></div>则臣今日之去就，固可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169380_comment'></div>向者，臣得待罪于宪司，不能谏正朝廷之失，同时言事之臣，皆被窜逐，而臣独留而不去，固已得罪于古人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169380_comment'></div>方斯时也，其惟辞大以就小，辞富以居贫，岂宜更冒恩荣，不度于义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169380_comment'></div>自闻除目之下，宠数便蕃，中外闻之，莫不惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169380_comment'></div>皆谓臣之顾惜利禄，言事依违，善承人主之意，有以得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169380_comment'></div>事虽不然，顾其迹，乌得使人不疑至此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169380_comment'></div>故口言之，心不存之，则人不信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169380_comment'></div>心存之，身不行之，则人不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169380_comment'></div>此臣今日之去就，正在乎力行于身，而求合于义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169380_comment'></div>《易》曰：「莫益之，或系之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169380_comment'></div>立心勿常，凶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169380_comment'></div>臣之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169380_comment'></div>况乎典诰之文，所以宣布王命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169380_comment'></div>劝讲经籍之义，所以开悟圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169380_comment'></div>今也言不足以见用于前，身不足以为法于后，且欲望其号令孚天下，而道义信人主，其可得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169380_comment'></div>故臣之所以不敢承命者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169380_comment'></div>所有前件敕三道，并未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169380_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，早赐追寝施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169380_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1169380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《辞直舍人院判吏部流内铨兼天章阁侍讲状》<div id='poem_1169380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞直舍人院兼判吏部流内铨兼天章阁侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169380")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169380'>臣近尝有状敷奏，辞免直舍人院及兼判吏部流内铨兼天章阁侍讲恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169380_comment'></div>今月十二日，准中书劄子，奉圣旨不许辞免，仰便受敕牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169380_comment'></div>今月十三日，延和殿侍立，又蒙内臣传宣，召臣面谕圣旨，令臣受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169380_comment'></div>臣虽再三辞避，不蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169380_comment'></div>又以侍讲之命，前来已降，御批宣谕，责臣以经义之益，亦令勿辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169380_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，上荷圣恩之厚，皇恐之际，难以固违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169380_comment'></div>退而思之，终是义理未安，不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169380_comment'></div>故臣区区之诚，尚有未尽者，不避罪戮，须至再烦天听，惟陛下俯加察允，则愚臣幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169380_comment'></div>臣闻之，君子之仕，行其义也，非以为利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169380_comment'></div>夫所谓义者，食其食而忧其事，不以一身之所利，而忘天下之所患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169380_comment'></div>道之行也，言之从也，虽禄之以万钟而不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169380_comment'></div>道之不行也，言之不从也，则致为臣而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169380_comment'></div>此古人之所以去就也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169380_comment'></div>今也中国一君，内外莫非其臣，舍乎是，则夷狄之国，无可去之义矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169380_comment'></div>故其道之不行，言之不用，乌乎之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169380_comment'></div>必也辞尊以居卑，辞富以居贫，辞内以居外，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169380_comment'></div>则臣今日之去就，固可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169380_comment'></div>向者，臣得待罪于宪司，不能谏正朝廷之失，同时言事之臣，皆被窜逐，而臣独留而不去，固已得罪于古人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169380_comment'></div>方斯时也，其惟辞大以就小，辞富以居贫，岂宜更冒恩荣，不度于义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169380_comment'></div>自闻除目之下，宠数便蕃，中外闻之，莫不惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169380_comment'></div>皆谓臣之顾惜利禄，言事依违，善承人主之意，有以得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169380_comment'></div>事虽不然，顾其迹，乌得使人不疑至此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169380_comment'></div>故口言之，心不存之，则人不信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169380_comment'></div>心存之，身不行之，则人不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169380_comment'></div>此臣今日之去就，正在乎力行于身，而求合于义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169380_comment'></div>《易》曰：「莫益之，或系之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169380_comment'></div>立心勿常，凶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169380_comment'></div>臣之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169380_comment'></div>况乎典诰之文，所以宣布王命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169380_comment'></div>劝讲经籍之义，所以开悟圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169380_comment'></div>今也言不足以见用于前，身不足以为法于后，且欲望其号令孚天下，而道义信人主，其可得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169380_comment'></div>故臣之所以不敢承命者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169380_comment'></div>所有前件敕三道，并未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169380_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，早赐追寝施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169380_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1169380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《辞修起居注状》<div id='poem_1169381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞修起居注状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169381")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169381'>臣窃闻已有圣旨，除臣守本官，充秘阁校理，修起居注者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169381_comment'></div>叨恩至厚，感惕交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169381_comment'></div>伏念臣本性至愚，学非深造，向者误蒙恩奖，擢置台端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169381_comment'></div>惟知忠以爱君，岂顾言之获戾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169381_comment'></div>方属朝廷更事，物议沸腾，身处法官，义当论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169381_comment'></div>识浅难周于事体，言轻莫悟于圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169381_comment'></div>陛下深示矜容，未加谴斥，只解横床之职，俾还内史之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169381_comment'></div>虽鸿造之曲全，在愚臣而难处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169381_comment'></div>臣近尝面奏，以言事不职，不敢久妨贤路，尚处宪司，愿乞外官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169381_comment'></div>已蒙俞旨，更居近列，诚所未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169381_comment'></div>欲望圣慈，令臣只守本官，归馆供职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169381_comment'></div>或除江淮一小郡，庶申愚效，上答眷知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169381_comment'></div>所有修起居注敕命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169381_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1169381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《择日祗受修起居注敕命状》<div id='poem_1169382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>择日祗受修起居注敕命状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169382")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169382'>臣今月二十六日，亲事官张潜赍到内降封还臣所辞避修起居注奏状，</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1169382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《秘阁校理修起居注举自代状》<div id='poem_1169367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秘阁校理修起居注举自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169367")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169367'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169367'>臣伏见前授忠武军节度推官、知许州长社县事常秩，学通于经，行信乎道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169367_comment'></div>使校秘文以备述作，或专直笔以载起居，臣实不如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169367_comment'></div>今举自代，谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1169367_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《辞兼天章阁侍讲状》<div id='poem_1169379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞兼天章阁侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169379")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169379'>臣今月十一日閤门告报，已降敕命，差臣兼天章阁侍讲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169379_comment'></div>宠数骤加，震惶无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169379_comment'></div>荷陛下之恩至厚，于臣子之分极荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169379_comment'></div>臣虽愚甚，非不能上体圣心，亟承明命，但以受之之际，义有未安，此臣不得而不辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169379_comment'></div>臣近以备位宪官，亦尝言时政之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169379_comment'></div>陛下不以臣言为可用，特令解职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169379_comment'></div>臣不能去，乃是废官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169379_comment'></div>上孤陛下任使之恩，下失人臣去就之义，岂可忘其忧责，更冒宠荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169379_comment'></div>而况侍讲禁中，盖老师大儒之任，非其道足以根诚明之本，学足以通伦类之变，其能发明经义之奥，以开导人主之德哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169379_comment'></div>如臣之愚，固不足以知此，且欲冒而居之，则是茍于利而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169379_comment'></div>夫怀利以事陛下，岂臣之心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169379_comment'></div>孟轲曰：「人亦孰不欲富贵，而独于富贵之中，有私龙断焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169379_comment'></div>人皆以为贱丈夫，亦臣之所不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169379_comment'></div>所有先降直舍人院敕，已有恳章辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169379_comment'></div>与今来所降恩命，伏望陛下察其心而特赐追寝，则愚臣之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169379_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169379_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《弹李南公除京西运判不当状》<div id='poem_1169392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹李南公除京西运判不当状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169392")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169392'>臣伏准中书劄子，太常博士李南公已降敕命就差权发遣京西路转运判官，依旧提举本路常平广惠仓，兼管勾农田水利差役事，劄付御史台者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169392_comment'></div>南公资力甚浅，学术无闻，虽小有才，不足以骤加剧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169392_comment'></div>近为制置司奏辟，专以青苗之法为便，迎合柄臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169392_comment'></div>曾未赴官，遽迁此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169392_comment'></div>虽理权发遣资序，其实与转运使副事权均一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169392_comment'></div>使廉按一路，所系不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169392_comment'></div>非素有资望之人，岂宜越次轻授？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169392_comment'></div>况青苗取利之法，臣已累次论列，乞行罢寝，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169392_comment'></div>今来更令转运判官专领其事，外持使者之权，内与制置司相为响应，足以公行率剥，坐致馀赢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169392_comment'></div>在于爱民，诚为未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169392_comment'></div>所有南公转运判官之命，欲乞追还，别与差遣，试之以事，如其的有显效，然后擢而任之，庶使轻扬巧佞之人，无由妄进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169392_comment'></div>仍乞以臣前后乞罢青苗劄子，早赐降付中书裁决施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169392_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169392_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《乞召还范纯仁状》<div id='poem_1169389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞召还范纯仁状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169389")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169389'>臣伏睹近降中书劄子内圣旨，就差知河中府、兵部员外郎、直集贤院范纯仁充成都府路转运使，劄付御史台者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169389_comment'></div>比闻御史中丞吕公著、右正言知谏院孙觉，皆有文字，乞留纯仁要剧差遣，未蒙俞旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169389_comment'></div>纯仁向以谏官，言事议论，有所不合，于义难处，恳求外官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169389_comment'></div>陛下深示矜容，不获已，而与之善郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169389_comment'></div>中外之论，已惜其去，谓无岁月之久，必当召还供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169389_comment'></div>今复使之远适，人情殊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169389_comment'></div>在陛下之意，不过藉其风力，安慰远民，然内外资望之臣，可以当此一路者，犹足选择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169389_comment'></div>如纯仁者，忠义劲正，乃陛下耳目之官，尝以言事被逐，而志无所夺，轻利信道，不为茍且之计，求之今日，岂易得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169389_comment'></div>众口一辞，皆以为不当去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169389_comment'></div>伏望圣意，早赐召归要近，以厌人望，非特臣之私言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169389_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《弹御史里行王子韶状》<div id='poem_1169404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹监察御史里行王子韶状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169404")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169404'>臣伏见监察御史里行王子韶，素非端士，滥处法官，阴附大臣，密通简札。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169404_comment'></div>访闻其兄子琦，预宫官之荐，子渊被提举之辟，尽由子韶私谒得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169404_comment'></div>臣窃以大臣之责，专以保任贤能，御史之职，在于纠绳非法，而乃卖恩请谒，同于市道，上下若兹，公义安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169404_comment'></div>欲乞取问制置司臣僚，子渊既是御史之兄，不知何人所荐，特宜推劾，以正罔上之刑，使今后近臣，不敢妄有奏辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169404_comment'></div>所有子韶回邪反覆，台中难与议事，伏望出自宸衷，别与差遣，庶清宪台，以塞人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169404_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1169404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《弹步军副都指挥使宋守约》三状。<div id='poem_1169406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹步军副指挥使宋守约状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169406")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169406'>臣访闻侍卫亲军步军副都指挥使、威武军节度观察留后、管勾都指挥使公事宋守约，为性贪暴，违越不公，陵虐军人，非理鞭配，前后私役军士修盖第宅物业，日不减一二百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169406_comment'></div>及分布东西窑灶，变造塼甓，津般土木，以至脱堑打草之类，莫非军人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169406_comment'></div>道途怨嗟，无敢言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169406_comment'></div>居陛下手足下，而敢恣横如此，其可容乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169406_comment'></div>伏望陛下以臣之言，取责诸军人员，即见逐件事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169406_comment'></div>褫职诏狱，以正典刑，庶使今后管军臣僚，不敢违越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169406_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1169406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论差择县令劄子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论流内铨奏辟属官劄子》<div id='poem_1169418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论流内铨奏辟属官劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169418")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169418'>臣伏见流内铨差注选人引用编敕及本司专一条贯，多是该说事理不尽，须至检寻前后体例，比附施行，然其间或一事而有数例，轻重不一，主判官既不尽知，则只由吏人检到为定，此铨衡用例之大弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169418_comment'></div>又本铨与南曹积年行遣要用文字，浩穰万计，虽置库贮，自来不曾编排架阁，绝不整齐，并格式一司，最为多事，专掌天下员阙与支遣选人料钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169418_comment'></div>勾凿簿书，编录条贯，虽事属南曹，自来无官点检，只是委凭吏人主管，欺弊极多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169418_comment'></div>窃闻朝廷近议，在京官府，并置属官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169418_comment'></div>臣欲乞从本司同罪奏辟历任有举主无私过京官或选人两员，素有才望可以济务者，充主簿或编修条例名目，专委管勾铨曹逐司文字，编排架阁，及提点格式司支遣料钱，入凿阙簿，并将凭由照对，躬亲印押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169418_comment'></div>及应是前后应用诸般体例文字，尽令类聚编录，委无漏落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169418_comment'></div>责自本司与判曹官员，同共看详，除不可用者合行删去外，其馀条目虽多、轻重不一，可以兼存者，并乞编为例册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169418_comment'></div>奏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1169418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论差选京朝官知县劄子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《弹秀州军事判官李定状》<div id='poem_1169405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹秀州军事判官李定状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169405")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169405'>臣窃以任人之术，莫大于分别邪正，而知君子小人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169405_comment'></div>君子之道好义，而不顾其利，故其言也忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169405_comment'></div>小人之道好利，而不顾其义，故其言也佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169405_comment'></div>此君人者，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169405_comment'></div>伏见秀州军事判官李定，近为右正言孙觉所荐，被召赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169405_comment'></div>定知天下之人皆以青苗之法为非，而独王安石之徒主以为是，每游安石之门，及与士大夫言，莫不盛称青苗之法，以为仁政，欲以迎合安石之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169405_comment'></div>前日窃闻已被召对，定之口才便佞，必能为甘言以悦陛下之心，仍虑制置司臣僚，喜其附己，阴相引荐，置之要路，以乱大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169405_comment'></div>又闻定与人言，陛下已曾面许台谏任使，事虽未然，或虑陛下知之未深，误有进用，似此谀佞之人，非朝廷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169405_comment'></div>孔子曰：「远佞人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169405_comment'></div>荀卿曰：「谄谀我者，吾贼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169405_comment'></div>斯至论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169405_comment'></div>所有臣近尝弹奏太常博士李南公资序至浅，小才善佞，乞追还转运判官之命，又言监察御史王子韶回邪反覆，难与议事，及定阿谀不正，并望别与外任合入差遣，庶绝佞人侥倖之路，而不误陛下任使之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169405_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《乞止绝权贵陈乞恩例劄子》<div id='poem_1169424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞止绝权贵非次陈乞恩例劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169424")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169424'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169424'>臣窃见近日臣寮并故臣寮之家，陈乞内外亲属恩泽，冲改已授差遣人员阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169424_comment'></div>朝廷虽有先降指挥，过一月之外不许冲改，然所陈乞恩例，名目稍多，逐时中书、枢密院不住于审官三班院流内铨取已使员阙差注，终属未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169424_comment'></div>缘逐处待阙之人，守候名次，动经岁月，洎至授下差遣，出京待阙，或已前去赴任，却被冲改，虽在远方，不免依前再赴铨院别候阙次，孤寒久旅之人，宁不嗟怨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169424_comment'></div>朝廷既有恩例，许令指射优便差遣，已是优恩，岂可更容冲夺已使员阙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169424_comment'></div>甚无谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169424_comment'></div>兼陈乞恩泽，多是近上臣僚之家，非理侥求，因成体例，攀援引用，寖不可革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169424_comment'></div>国家爵禄恩赏，所以待贤能之士，今惟以父兄亲属私恩陈乞，使阀阅无功之人，占夺优便差遣，一切出于侥倖，甚非至公之朝慎名重器、区别能否之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169424_comment'></div>臣以为立法更弊，必先自贵者始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169424_comment'></div>欲乞今后除前两府出镇与沿边安抚帅臣辟举人，依条施行，及劳绩酬奖堂除人，许指射非次见阙外，其馀乞先自两府以至文武臣僚及分司致仕故臣僚之家，如合陈乞弟侄儿男及异姓骨肉恩泽，并奏荐人差遣等，并令一例于季阙以前一月内指挥合入优便之处，依例等待，即不得临时陈乞非次见阙，及冲改已授差遣人员阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169424_comment'></div>庶使权贵绝侥求之望，寒士无被夺之患，而稍获均济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169424_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论散青苗不便乞住支》五状。<div id='poem_1169362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论散青苗不便乞住支状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169362")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169362'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169362'>臣伏见制置三司条例司奏辟属官提举管勾诸路常平广惠仓俵散青苗钱斛事，其劄子元降指挥，预俵之法，本以为民，而公家无所利其入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169362_comment'></div>至于敛散之际，亦皆取人之便，而不得抑配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169362_comment'></div>盖取先王耕敛补助之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169362_comment'></div>今来风闻诸路所遣提举管勾官，多不体认元降指挥，凭藉事权，陵压州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169362_comment'></div>却以青苗之法，取民利息二分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169362_comment'></div>等第之家，不问其愿与不愿，一例抑配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169362_comment'></div>物论喧然，以为骚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169362_comment'></div>窃缘朝廷之意，本为小民阙乏，常在于新陈不接之际，倍息举贷，以取资给，故设青苗预支之法，使农人得以资助耕敛，而兼并不得以乘其急，是欲专以便民，而非有以规其利也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169362_comment'></div>今使者一出，而天下之人皆谓朝廷只以补助之说为名，而其实专在于取息而已，是岂立法之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169362_comment'></div>苟朝廷之法不然，而使者为之，致陛下失大惠于民，则辱命之罪莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169362_comment'></div>宜正典刑以示天下，使中外晓然知陛下孚惠之心，非有取利于百姓可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169362_comment'></div>如朝廷立法之初，果以为利，则不特有司之过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169362_comment'></div>为父而榷其子，此汉武之事，非陛下所宜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169362_comment'></div>不惟不可行，时亦不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169362_comment'></div>将以惠民，适所以害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169362_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169362_comment'></div>比岁以来，四方多事，河决地震，水潦民饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169362_comment'></div>陕右有备边之须，河朔有修城之役，民力凋敝，疮痍未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169362_comment'></div>天下无名之敛，所在有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169362_comment'></div>如闻诸路之民，尚有积年逋负官物，动以万计，未能输入，今更以青苗取利，人必不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169362_comment'></div>不惟重以困民，适足害其官本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169362_comment'></div>大率小人见利，幸于茍得，既用之后，多不能偿，大者须至于逋逃，小者不免于刑辟，此必然之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169362_comment'></div>臣前谓将以惠民，适所以害之者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169362_comment'></div>臣欲乞早降指挥，下诸路提点刑狱司，更切体量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169362_comment'></div>差去提举管勾常平钱斛官员，内有生事，擅违朝旨，特与减黜施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169362_comment'></div>其青苗钱已行支俵者，将来只令随税送纳本钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169362_comment'></div>如未俵散处，并令罢支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169362_comment'></div>庶不失陷官本钱，及别致骚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169362_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1169362_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论青苗钱第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169363")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169363'>臣近有奏状，为诸路俵散青苗钱官员内有生事扰民、擅违朝旨，乞特与减黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169363_comment'></div>及青苗已行俵散者，只令送纳本钱，如未俵散处，并令罢支等事，未蒙朝旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169363_comment'></div>窃详条例司元降指挥，以常平、广惠变为青苗之法，申严赏罚，督责州县，以谨其给纳，虽以优民救乏为名，其实不异民间举放之事，以渔民取利而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169363_comment'></div>岂陛下圣明之主所宜为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169363_comment'></div>就使国家帑藏空虚，财用不足，亦未至经纪小民，放本取利，事体削弱，如此之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169363_comment'></div>今来访闻诸路所差官吏，为见朝廷属意财利，莫不望风希旨，务为诛剥，以觊幸酬赏，茍免黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169363_comment'></div>或以三分取息，或将陈旧之物，纽作贵价兑换支散，或不以民之贫富，一例抑配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169363_comment'></div>事初如此，其后可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169363_comment'></div>臣恐此法一行，骚动天下，希锥刀之利，失亿兆之心，胎祸之端，未必不由兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169363_comment'></div>况兴事改法，系国家安危大计，上有公卿谋议，下有台谏纠绳，岂可只由条例一司独专其事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169363_comment'></div>置陛下于有过，使黎元之不安，茍利一时，敛怨天下，非细事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169363_comment'></div>臣欲乞将中外臣僚前后上言常平青苗等不便事件章疏，并臣前状，降付中书，令与密院一处看详，定夺可否，及下两制臣僚，共析利害闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169363_comment'></div>庶陛下得以尽天下之公议，知事体之难行，特赐寝罢，以安人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169363_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1169363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169363'><span class='label'>按：</span>《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一一一题作「上神宗论青苗」。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1169363_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1169364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论青苗钱第三状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169364")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169364'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169364'>臣闻臣之事君，有犯无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169364_comment'></div>夫犯颜忤旨，以取君父之怒，岂其所欲哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169364_comment'></div>盖义有可言而不言，非爱君之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169364_comment'></div>此臣所以昧死而不敢隐默者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169364_comment'></div>臣近以青苗之法，骚扰不便，欲乞寝罢，以安人心，未蒙俞旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169364_comment'></div>陛下圣性聪明，固已晓然开悟，但以王安石执议不变，重违其情，物论喧然，不加听察，事之可者则置而勿问，其不可者则无所不行，岂非条例之臣为自安之计，巧为饰说，诬罔圣聪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169364_comment'></div>近者韩琦上言，以河北俵散青苗钱，立定贯伯，均与等第人户，比之他路，独取息三分，显是提举之官违条抑配，而朝廷并无黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169364_comment'></div>琦之论列，足以知其非便，而特寝不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169364_comment'></div>吕景以畿县之民，逋负官物，尚有五十馀万，不宜更与预支，实亏陷官本，而却令取勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169364_comment'></div>夫擅行抑配者，既无罪黜，则掊克之吏，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169364_comment'></div>不忍为骚扰者，反蒙按劾，则民之司牧，何所措其手足哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169364_comment'></div>故臣前曰：「此法一行，骚动天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169364_comment'></div>正谓此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169364_comment'></div>陛下近以司马光为枢密副使，中外翕然，皆以陛下知光之言为是，而悟制置司之为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169364_comment'></div>今复遽然罢之者，岂又以光言为非邪，必以其辞而不受也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169364_comment'></div>然则光之所以不受者，以陛下不行其言尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169364_comment'></div>知其言而不用，犹可以去，又况有所受命乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169364_comment'></div>如欲用之，行其言而已矣，何吝而不为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169364_comment'></div>轻进退于大臣，失孚号于天下，非所谓令出弗反之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169364_comment'></div>李常职在谏官，既闻中外之议，不敢不言，事虽不实，诚亦得之舆论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169364_comment'></div>况国朝旧制，自许风闻言事，若令分析，是欲使其必去，将以杜言者之口，恐非所以待谏臣之体而广言路之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169364_comment'></div>凡此数事，虽圣虑一时之失，岂非听者之误乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169364_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「有所忿懥，则不得其正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169364_comment'></div>有所好乐，则不得其正」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169364_comment'></div>亦在陛下追而正之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169364_comment'></div>《书》曰「改过不吝」，汤之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169364_comment'></div>自陛下临政以来，事无过举，惟用安石，然后有更事之暴，而致兴利之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169364_comment'></div>圣人施为，自有法度，合于道者取之，不合于道者去之，任天下之群才，取天下之公议，尧舜三王之治，可以指期而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169364_comment'></div>又何必徇一士之曲议，以贻黎元之患哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169364_comment'></div>所有制置条例司，如有可行事件，欲乞只归三司相度施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169364_comment'></div>青苗之法，早赐停寝，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169364_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1169364_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论青苗钱第四状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169365")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169365'>臣近尝三次上言，论列青苗之法，乞行寝罢，而陛下未以臣言为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169365_comment'></div>臣得待罪于言事之官，凡时政之阙失，近于苛细，犹得斥而言之，顾此一事，最为害政之大者，茍依违不言，置陛下于有过之地，则臣上负朝廷任使之意，不忠之罪莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169365_comment'></div>臣观制置司元降指挥，莫非引经以为言，而其实贷民以取利，事体削弱，为天下讥笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169365_comment'></div>是特为管仲、商君之术，非陛下之所宜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169365_comment'></div>臣愿陛下为尧舜之君，以仁义治天下，不愿其为霸主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169365_comment'></div>昔者伊尹不俾厥后为尧舜，其心愧耻，若挞于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169365_comment'></div>是以高宗命说曰：「尔尚明保予，罔俾阿衡专美有商」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169365_comment'></div>古之人其责难于君如此之备，而又肯逢君以利而为霸者之术哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169365_comment'></div>夫所谓霸者，当战国之时，诸侯之土地皆褊小而不足，上无圣贤之君，下无王者之臣，而外有敌国之患，计出于不获已而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169365_comment'></div>管仲以区区之齐，居于海滨，于是兼鱼盐之利，权重轻之法，假仁义而行谲诈，欲以强国足兵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169365_comment'></div>然而不能使其君为王政，此圣门之所耻言，而曾西所以卑其功烈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169365_comment'></div>商鞅之事秦也，说其君以强国之术，故变法令，开阡陌，信赏罚，而秦人莫敢不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169365_comment'></div>然而谓其君不可与入尧舜之道，此正孟轲所谓「谓其君不能，贼其君者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169365_comment'></div>彼二子者，使知以仁义事其君，而行王者之政，其肯茍一时之利，以贻天下万世之讥哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169365_comment'></div>臣故曰：霸者盖国小而力不足，上无圣贤之君，下无王者之臣，而外有敌国之患，计出于不获已而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169365_comment'></div>方今陛下富有中国，广轮万里，上有贤圣之君，下有王者之臣，内无强臣敌国之患，外无西戎北狄之难，凡四海九州之赋入，又足以供吾之用，而不为不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169365_comment'></div>陛下不于此时与庙堂之臣坐而论道，以行王政，而反屑屑为均输、举贷之事，臣窃为陛下惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169365_comment'></div>然则今日之弊，在于国家因循，制度未立，而侈用日广，斯亦不足患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169365_comment'></div>陛下但慎选主计之臣，付与利柄，取天下赋入之籍，度县官调度之数，百用为之均节，而归之艺极，则浮费省而财用足，斯可以行王政矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169365_comment'></div>省徭役，薄赋敛，则天下之农，不释耒而耕矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169365_comment'></div>宽关市之征，弛山泽之禁，则天下之商，不藏镪而行矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169365_comment'></div>修庠序之教，劝之以忠信孝悌，则天下之民，皆遣其子弟而兴于学矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169365_comment'></div>尊贤而使能，才者进，不才者退，则天下之士，皆励其德行而为良吏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169365_comment'></div>农有馀粟，商有馀财，民服其教，吏称其职，然而国不富而政不王者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169365_comment'></div>子贡曰：「文武之道，未坠于地，在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169365_comment'></div>贤者识其大者，不贤者识其小者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169365_comment'></div>夫道亦在择焉而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169365_comment'></div>惟陛下舍乎兴利之道，而行乎保民之政，则圣人之治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169365_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1169365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论青苗钱第五状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169366")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169366'>臣近以青苗之法，骚民为害，欲乞寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169366_comment'></div>其制置司立法之误，中外言者已详，臣固不复一一论列，上烦圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169366_comment'></div>但以方今天下，生民困弊，财力殚竭，二税之外，更有无名科率，何啻十色有馀，若复俵散青苗钱，实恐民不堪命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169366_comment'></div>陛下以至仁求治，凡欲更张法度，皆以为民，安有取民脂膏，以为贷息，而谓周公太平已试之法哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169366_comment'></div>陛下之心必不为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169366_comment'></div>然则天下之人，皆知误陛下者，王安石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169366_comment'></div>误安石者，吕惠卿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169366_comment'></div>以陛下之聪明，观天下之论议，其法利害，固已灼然可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169366_comment'></div>奈何安石持强辩以荧惑于前，惠卿画诡谋以阴助于后，加以反覆比周之小人，随时观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169366_comment'></div>平日公论，则举知其法之非，一揉于利，则又言其法之是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169366_comment'></div>此虽陛下之至圣，不能无惑，虽臣等之至忠，亦不免指为朋党也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169366_comment'></div>近者，谏官李常以言事待罪，尚令分析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169366_comment'></div>孙觉以奏对反覆，落职外迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169366_comment'></div>御史中丞吕公著而下，皆以不职为言，乞从责降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169366_comment'></div>而臣独区区未敢以请者，尚冀犬马之诚，一悟圣意，许以青苗之法，下议百官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169366_comment'></div>如臣等之言非，则甘从远窜，以戒妄言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169366_comment'></div>如臣等之言是，则安石、惠卿亦允特行贬斥，以谢天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169366_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169366'><span class='label'>《国朝诸臣奏议》文后有小字注：</span>「熙宁三年四月上，时为侍御史知杂事。既而有旨召襄试知制诰于中书，襄以言不行，辞不就试，乞补外，王安石请用为集贤殿修撰、陕西转运使，命未下，上批别进云，遂罢知杂事，为同修起居注。」<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1169366_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论李常待罪不报及吕公著落职劄子》<div id='poem_1169419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李常待罪不报及吕公著落职劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169419")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169419'>臣闻之孔子曰：「君使臣以礼，臣事君以忠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169419_comment'></div>伏见右正言李常，以经行为陛下所知，擢自稠人之中，寘之谏诤之列，可谓待之礼优矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169419_comment'></div>常以受恩思报，不敢爱身避事，知青苗取利之为害，不免论列其非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169419_comment'></div>观常之心，固已尽忠于陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169419_comment'></div>向者止以一言之过，便令分析，居家待罪，两月而不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169419_comment'></div>人情疑惑，皆谓陛下待常之礼已薄，而不欲以无名逐之，俟其抵触忌讳，自取罪尤而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169419_comment'></div>此必非陛下之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169419_comment'></div>岂有天子任耳目之官，而罗织语言之过，将以为罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169419_comment'></div>虽曰行法，其能弭人之言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169419_comment'></div>此乃学黄老刑名者之所为，怵陛下以为此，恐非忠厚之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169419_comment'></div>近闻御史中丞吕公著，亦以造膝之言，落职补郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169419_comment'></div>参知政事王安石增改诰词，暴扬其语，欲以中伤公著，且以杜藩臣之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169419_comment'></div>传播四方，深失事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169419_comment'></div>所可惜者，陛下刑赏之柄，岂得出于制置之臣，台谏去就之命，不当制于仇人之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169419_comment'></div>夫忠言逆耳，不幸而有过，陛下逐之可也，杀之可也，又何憾焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169419_comment'></div>如使权臣得以专之，此天下之所不服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169419_comment'></div>况今台谏之臣，待罪相继，臣之论列，事体颇同，虽陛下未废其言，尚令就职，若青苗之法未罢，臣等义必难留，殛之窜之，惟陛下早赐裁决，无使强臣得以专制其命，则臣等之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169419_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论王安石劄子》<div id='poem_1169426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王安石劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169426")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169426'>臣窃以天下之道常存乎公议，公议废，斯道或几乎熄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169426_comment'></div>夫人皆有是非可否之心，盖出于理义之性，虽圣人无以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169426_comment'></div>方其是非可否之时，茍其心不至乎有所好恶，则其言未始不公，虽匹夫匹妇之愚，犹有可取，而况士君子者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169426_comment'></div>彼君民者，凡施一政，立一事，方且自谓吾思虑之甚精，议论之甚熟，闻其言而莫之省也，且以为流俗之论，亦不思之甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169426_comment'></div>故天下之公议，常起于好恶未发之前，而失于是非相胜之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169426_comment'></div>君人者，不可不察乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169426_comment'></div>己以为是而天下以为非，己以为非而天下以为是焉，未可也，必待天下之人皆以为非，然后舍焉，是众人舍之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169426_comment'></div>故其取于人也，无贵贱戚疏贤愚，惟恐其谋之者不多，论之者不博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169426_comment'></div>道之所存，议之所从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169426_comment'></div>古者，天子听政，使公卿至于列士献诗，瞽献曲，史献书，师箴，瞍赋，矇诵，百工谏，庶人传语，近臣尽规，亲戚补察，瞽、史教诲，耆、艾修之，而后王斟酌焉，是以事行而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1169426", 1169426, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>不悖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169426_comment'></div>厉王暴虐，使人监谤，召公用是谏之而不听，遂至流亡之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169426_comment'></div>宣王既立，用周、召以为辅相，修文、武、成、康之遗风，而雅道复行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169426_comment'></div>故其政善者，诗人美之，若《云汉》、《崧高》之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169426_comment'></div>其不善者，诗人亦或箴焉，《庭燎》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169426_comment'></div>或规焉，《沔水》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169426_comment'></div>或诲焉，《鹤鸣》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169426_comment'></div>或刺焉，《祈父》、《白驹》之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169426_comment'></div>故天下诸侯复宗周而王室中兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169426_comment'></div>夫言之于人君，其取舍兴亡如此之明效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169426_comment'></div>伏自陛下享国以来，咨嗟求治，惟恐一言之不获，一事之未闻，亲降诏书，询求阙政，每遇便殿，延访群臣之言，至于日昃，仍命百寮转对，得以封事上闻，求之前王，未有陛下兼收广听如此之勤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169426_comment'></div>然而兴事改作，惟圣其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169426_comment'></div>王安石者，道德之臣，经艺明诚，足以开导人主，不当责以有司财利之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169426_comment'></div>近置条例一司，失于过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169426_comment'></div>事不由于宰府，谋不及于士民，耆艾不与闻，台谏不得议，所建议者，惟门生属吏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169426_comment'></div>天下虽有是非之论，一切不听，事行之日，中外莫不悱然非之，谓不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169426_comment'></div>此由责任太专，而不取人言之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169426_comment'></div>《易》之《蛊》曰：「先甲三日，后甲三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169426_comment'></div>终则有始，天行也者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169426_comment'></div>言有事而待能之时，人君欲创制申令，必先慎虑于始，又当图成其终，犹天道之行四时以成变化，奈何独以一二臣之臆见而议天下之法哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169426_comment'></div>陛下虽欲从之，其如天下何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169426_comment'></div>昔者子产相郑，郑人有游乡校以论执政者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169426_comment'></div>然明请毁乡校，子产止之，曰：「夫人朝夕退而游焉，以议执政之善否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169426_comment'></div>其所善者，吾则行之，其所恶者，吾则改之，是吾师也，若之何毁之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169426_comment'></div>孔子闻之曰：「人谓子产不仁，吾不信也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169426_comment'></div>韩愈为之颂曰：「诚率是道，相天下君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169426_comment'></div>旁通交畅，施及无垠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169426_comment'></div>盖惜其不遇也，又曰：「四海所以不治，有君无臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169426_comment'></div>谁其嗣之，我思古人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169426_comment'></div>盖伤今不复有斯人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169426_comment'></div>伏望陛下复雅道以行宣王之政，责近臣以子产之用心，无任一人之私言，无废天下之公论，举一事必稽于众，施一政必顺于民，罢去诛求之法以安人心，牵复放斥之臣以开言路，使百工群吏咸得以职事持议箴补王阙，则可以无偏系过举之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169426_comment'></div>《易》曰：「同人于野，亨，利涉大川」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169426_comment'></div>言所同者远，无所系吝，则道光亨，可济大事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169426_comment'></div>伏惟陛下留神听纳，则天下之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169426_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1169426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论韩维充侍御中丞与韩绛领制置司妨碍状》<div id='poem_1169390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论韩维充御史中丞与韩绛领制置司妨碍状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169390")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169390'>臣窃闻御史中丞吕公著以言事待罪，蒙恩解职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169390_comment'></div>已有圣旨除翰林学士韩维充御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169390_comment'></div>方公著待罪之初，议者纷纷，皆谓朝廷既不用公著之言，必与制置司为地，求其所与，以备宪司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169390_comment'></div>今既以维代之，乃是陛下选用正人，未为壅塞言路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169390_comment'></div>然枢密副使韩绛，见领制置三司条例司事，是维之兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169390_comment'></div>弹奏之间，不无妨碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169390_comment'></div>况今青苗之事未息，而言者不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169390_comment'></div>欲乞罢绛制置司事，使维得以论事无避，而亦足弭人之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169390_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1169390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄作《论韩绛参知政事乞罢制置司状》<div id='poem_1169391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论除韩绛参知政事乞罢制置司状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169391")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169391'>臣窃闻已有制命除枢密副使韩绛为参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169391_comment'></div>绛以才望序迁，固未为过，然朝廷所以用绛之意，似乎不厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169391_comment'></div>陛下始用王安石参预大政，首为兴利之谋，先与知枢密院事陈升之同领制置三司条例司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169391_comment'></div>未几，升之用是迁为丞相，而绛又领之，曾不数月，今又以绛参预政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169391_comment'></div>则是中书选任大臣，皆以利进，自古至治之朝，未有斯事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169391_comment'></div>《书》曰：「兹惟三公，论道经邦，燮理阴阳，官不必备，惟其人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169391_comment'></div>此辅相之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169391_comment'></div>太戊之兴也，则有伊陟臣扈，格于上帝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1169391", 1169391, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>巫咸</span>乂王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169391_comment'></div>高宗之兴也，则有甘盘、傅说，而商礼配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169391_comment'></div>成王之立也，则周公为师，召公为保，兴作礼乐，遂致太平之功，不闻以利责之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169391_comment'></div>唐宪宗刚明果断，能立事功，以藩镇渐平，肆意侈欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169391_comment'></div>程异、皇甫镈探知上旨，以诛剥财利悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169391_comment'></div>故宪宗独排物议，而以异、镈为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169391_comment'></div>裴度素所亲信，虽极言论列，终亦不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169391_comment'></div>季年昏惑，曾庸主之不若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169391_comment'></div>信乎，利之蔽人也如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169391_comment'></div>君人者之所任与其所好，足以为戒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169391_comment'></div>今陛下执政之臣，凡以利进者三人矣，虽圣德高明，不足以致惑，亦不可以不慎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169391_comment'></div>臣欲乞罢绛参知政事，今后中书选任大臣，必求道德经术之贤以处之，而不得以利进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169391_comment'></div>如陛下不欲追寝已行之命，即乞将制置条例司与青苗补助之法只归三司，及责之守令相度施行，庶不害于王政，而足以全大臣之节矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169391_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1169391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年秋</a>　秋，陈襄知制诰，迁尚书吏部郎中，兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　陈襄作《内制》一卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　陈襄作《谢知制诰启》<div id='poem_1169537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169537")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169537'>误被制恩，猥升辞禁，省躬非称，视宠逾惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169537_comment'></div>伏以朝廷号令之严，台阁文辞之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169537_comment'></div>浑然深厚，则涵泳乎人心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169537_comment'></div>涣然流行，则鼓舞乎天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169537_comment'></div>其命代言之士，必惟名世之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169537_comment'></div>矧属上圣有为，高视百王之制作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169537_comment'></div>异人间出，力追三代之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169537_comment'></div>语才为难，居此尤盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169537_comment'></div>自匪一时之杰，曷膺万选之功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169537_comment'></div>如某者，拙朴寡能，憃冥有志，学惟知于事道，才不善于趋时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169537_comment'></div>勉为禄仕而居贫，耻若狂夫之进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169537_comment'></div>早被近臣之荐，获陪延阁之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169537_comment'></div>丹笔雠书，甘心白首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169537_comment'></div>朱轓补郡，绝意青云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169537_comment'></div>适当龙德之飞，召对螭头之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169537_comment'></div>寻迁谏省，复贰宪司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169537_comment'></div>同时言事之臣，去者过半；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169537_comment'></div>平日爱君之志，知者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169537_comment'></div>盖常慕古人之皇皇，誓不为匹夫之悻悻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169537_comment'></div>人皆指以为利，己独信而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169537_comment'></div>宠恩便蕃，固已恳辞而不受；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169537_comment'></div>赐札训谕，虽欲亟去而非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169537_comment'></div>祗旧服以冒居，徒终年而无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169537_comment'></div>坐妨贤路，何逃糠秕之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169537_comment'></div>请假州符，想见江湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169537_comment'></div>岂谓盛时之际会，俯临晚节以甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169537_comment'></div>试其一日之长，置在群豪之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169537_comment'></div>此盖某官，立朝以道，事主以人，推致大公，激扬众善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169537_comment'></div>谓育才者，君子所乐，尝借先容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169537_comment'></div>谓进贤者，大臣之能，实资馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169537_comment'></div>敢不益敦名节，勉著事功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169537_comment'></div>期无失职之愆，仰答知人之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169537_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1169537_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f7c70f47ca60447cbc4454d8dbda8597_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f7c70f47ca60447cbc4454d8dbda8597");'><span id='f7c70f47ca60447cbc4454d8dbda8597_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1080')">1075-1080年</a>，59-64岁</div><div id='f7c70f47ca60447cbc4454d8dbda8597' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年冬</a>　冬，陈襄被召还京，知通进银台司，兼门下封驳事，提举进奏院，迁尚书右司郎中，枢密直学士，判太常寺，兼礼仪事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　陈襄作《论差除敕不由封驳司劄子》<div id='poem_1169428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论差除敕不由封駮司劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169428")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169428'>臣窃以封駮一司，乃朝廷慎出命令之关防也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169428_comment'></div>故凡宣敕之出，莫不由于门下者，盖虑政令有所未便，刑赏有所未中，差除有所未当，则有司得以看详而举駮是非，亦补朝政之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169428_comment'></div>近者，翰林学士、知通进银台司、兼门下封駮事范镇奏，为差提举广惠仓官员敕不下封駮司事，中书检会，为系举官，更不下封駮司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169428_comment'></div>以臣观之，夫举官任人，国之大典，万一有不当，义当駮奏，岂可与閒漫文字一例直降，不由所司？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169428_comment'></div>上废朝纲，下失官守，此近年已失之事，岂可按以为法哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169428_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后中书、枢密院，除閒漫机密事依例直发外，自馀事关朝政有所可否者，其宣敕并令降付门下封駮施行，庶不失祖宗之成宪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169428_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1169428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　陈襄作《谢转枢密直学士启》<div id='poem_1169535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转枢密直学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169535")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169535'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169535'>叨膺明命，进秩中枢，逡避靡遑，冒荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169535_comment'></div>伏念某赋材朴直，逢世休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169535_comment'></div>惟知以道徇身，窃慕古人之仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169535_comment'></div>不谓无功受禄，猥蒙真主之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169535_comment'></div>自叨窃于贱官，亦践更于方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169535_comment'></div>微典诰之文，以发挥圣训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169535_comment'></div>乏循良之政，以宣布上恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169535_comment'></div>敢意召还，未从幽黜，亲承训谕，骤沐甄升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169535_comment'></div>进密勿之近班，被便蕃之宠锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169535_comment'></div>望逾涯分，职有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169535_comment'></div>斯盖伏遇某官，名世钜儒，佐时元老，仁先当务，道在进贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169535_comment'></div>乐以至诚，思嘉鱼之与善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169535_comment'></div>縻之好爵，取鸣鹤之交孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169535_comment'></div>曾是孤生，亦尘华选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169535_comment'></div>敢不益坚名节，敦养诚明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169535_comment'></div>恭爱一于事君，宠利归之忘己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169535_comment'></div>庶尽拘儒之守，少酬知己之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169535_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169535_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈襄兼侍讲，知审官东院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈襄作《经筵荐温国司马公而下三十士章藁》一卷。<div id='poem_1169359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熙宁经筵论荐司马光等三十三人章藁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169359")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169359'>端明殿学士、右谏议大夫、集贤院修撰、提举西京嵩山崇福宫司马光，素有行实，忠亮正直，以道自任，博通书史之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169359_comment'></div>可备顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169359_comment'></div>端明殿学士、翰林院侍读学士、尚书吏部郎中、知许州韩维，器质方重，学亦醇正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169359_comment'></div>知尽心性理之说，得道于内，则可以应物于外矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169359_comment'></div>翰林侍读学士、宝文阁学士、尚书户部侍郎、提举西京嵩山崇福宫吕公著，道德醇明，学有原本，事君以进贤汲善为己任，可谓知务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169359_comment'></div>三人者，皆股肱心膂之臣，不当久外，乞诏还词苑，或居经帏，日侍燕闲，论思献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1169359'>学士有博学通典故者：秘书监、集贤院学士、知杭州苏颂，记问博洽，长于史学，国朝典故，多所练达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169359_comment'></div>所学，宋敏求之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169359_comment'></div>宜编撰检讨之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1169359'>馆职有学行器识可备侍从者：右司谏、直集贤院孙觉，素有乡行，明经术义理之学，端良信厚，可以镇浮厉世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169359_comment'></div>尚书祠部员外郎、秘阁校理、知齐州李常，性行醇正，兼治经术，久补外官，有循良之政，可比于觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169359_comment'></div>尚书兵部员外郎、直集贤院、知和州范纯仁，器识通明，忠义骨鲠，其才足以济大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169359_comment'></div>三人者皆可充近侍耳目之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1169359'>馆职有文学可为词臣者：尚书祠部员外郎、直史馆、权知河中府苏轼，豪俊端方，所学虽不长于经术，然子史百氏之书，无所不览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169359_comment'></div>文词美丽，擅于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169359_comment'></div>居官敏恕，尤通政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169359_comment'></div>尚书祠部员外郎、集贤校理、权知洪州曾巩，以文学名于时，人皆称其有才，然其文词近典雅，与轼之文各为一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169359_comment'></div>二人者皆词人之杰，可备文翰之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169359_comment'></div>祠部员外郎、集贤校理、同修起居注孙洙，博学能文，才识通敏，所守亦端，可充文翰史臣之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169359_comment'></div>兼明世务，通晓民政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169359_comment'></div>近蒙进擢修注，深厌士论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1169359'>馆职有学行端正可以擢居清要者：秘书丞、集贤校理王存，学行素著，方重有守，不为势利所迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169359_comment'></div>太子中允、馆阁校勘、判武学顾临，才豪而气刚，兼有识略，乐义尚贤，喜于闻过，可属以危难之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169359_comment'></div>秘书省著作佐郎、集贤校理林希，少有文行，明敏劲正，学亦该博，长于记问，可与编撰检讨之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1169359'>谪官未复职者：尚书右司郎中、分司南京李师中，人多称其有才，可当边帅之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169359_comment'></div>往岁近臣尝有论荐，其才它日为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169359_comment'></div>向因言事分务，若遂蠲洗，不惟责其后效，抑足以开言路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169359_comment'></div>尚书兵部员外郎傅尧俞，言事官以义去就，有古诤臣之风，不幸坐累褫职，未蒙牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169359_comment'></div>太常博士、新差河东路提点刑狱公事胡宗愈，文醇行循，兼明经术，东南人士，多所师服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169359_comment'></div>向以言事被谪，累经恩宥，未蒙复职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169359_comment'></div>前秘书省著作佐郎王安国，材器磊落，文亦豪迈，可充词翰之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169359_comment'></div>向居罪废间，不忘进学，亦奇伟之才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1169359'>京朝官、选人有学行才器可进擢台阁者：太子中允、馆阁校勘、签书应天府判官厅公事刘挚，性行端淳，词学渊远，若置之文馆，优游长育，必为远器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169359_comment'></div>太常博士、崇文院校书、勾当宗正丞公事虞太熙，治经有行，端方自守，不茍于进，可充台阁之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169359_comment'></div>太子中允、监西京洛河竹木务程颢，性行端醇，明于义理，可备风宪职司之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169359_comment'></div>太子中允、权发遣淮南西路转运判官公事刘载，少治经术，兼有文行，可备台阁之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169359_comment'></div>殿中丞、新差充秦凤熙河路措置边事司勾当公事兼催督军须薛昌朝，才质俱美，持守端直，当置台阁，以养其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169359_comment'></div>久从机宜之辟，非所以处之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169359_comment'></div>秘书省著作佐郎、崇文院校书张载，学行修明，养心事道，不茍仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169359_comment'></div>西方学者，如载一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169359_comment'></div>若稍加优宠，所劝大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169359_comment'></div>兴国军节度掌书记苏辙，其学与文，若不逮轼，而静厚过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169359_comment'></div>辙自登第及中制科，凡二十年，尚在选调，未蒙褒擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169359_comment'></div>前台州司户参军召试馆阁孔文仲，性醇行粹，如不能言，发为文章，温厚正直，稍加长育，必为瑰硕之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169359_comment'></div>新差歙州军事推官吴贲，端良质实，少以孝行闻于州乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169359_comment'></div>治《易》、《春秋》之学，而文亦淳雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169359_comment'></div>尤尽心于民政，所至以惠爱称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169359_comment'></div>前润州延陵县令吴恕，器识淳深，学通义理，若置之文馆，长育而成就之，可以与有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1169359'>常僚中才行器识可升擢任使者：尚书屯田郎中、知开封府太康县事林英，有才与行，安静详明，和而不随，直而无挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169359_comment'></div>尚书都官员外郎、监泗州河南转般仓孙奕，士行著于乡闾，节义信于朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169359_comment'></div>外虽朴淳，而中实强敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169359_comment'></div>英奕所至，皆以善政闻，可谓循良之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169359_comment'></div>使当一路，则可以厚风俗而安民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169359_comment'></div>秘书省著作佐郎、监扬州粮料院林旦，才力强明，通晓民政，兼有持守，可责任以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169359_comment'></div>太常博士、新差监衡州在城盐仓邹何，操履端方，吏材通敏，久居务局，士论惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1169359'>小臣言事黜废有可矜者：太子中允降授大理评事唐坰，性虽轻脱，然才干明敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169359_comment'></div>向以言事被窜，两经赦宥，初监广州军资库，次移监吉州太和县盐酒税，又次移监杭州龙山税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169359_comment'></div>流落远方，已是数年，愿特与亲民差遣，以来敢言之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169359_comment'></div>前光州司法参军、监安上门、英州安置勒停郑侠，向以狂言得罪，窜废海隅瘴疠之地，朝不保夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169359_comment'></div>小臣愚直敢言如此，是亦发于忠义，非陛下矜怜其志，而使得生还，谁复为侠言者<span class='inlineComment2'>（《古灵先生文集》卷一。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1169359'>正文前有司马光、韩维等三十三人姓名，今略。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1169359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈襄作《理会吏部资序劄子》<div id='poem_1169417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>理会吏部资序劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169417")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169417'>臣窃谓县有知令，最为亲民之官，不可一日虚其位，而或任非其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169417_comment'></div>臣所领审官东院契勘近日合入亲民资序官七十馀员，知县阙次八十馀处，全然差注不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169417_comment'></div>自新法以来，县道事繁，督责严密，被累者多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169417_comment'></div>故虽有廉良之才，稍知自重，则莫不畏罪规避，无敢就者，至有折资愿就閒局，此人情可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169417_comment'></div>今来任知县人不减五十馀员，并正任监当人又有九十馀员，其监当阙次只有十处，不惟县道阙人，兼监当待次人无由发遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169417_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞诏诸道监司长吏，今后县道官员，除庸谬不职，及委是故违新法，合行冲降外，自馀若非违越不职，偶因过不逮之人，少加容贷，原情薄责，使不至于黜降，则人人乐居其职，无或规避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169417_comment'></div>仍乞今后于元系亲民降充监当人内选择脚色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169417_comment'></div>如公罪及私罪杖以下，情理不至深重，历任曾有举主十人以上者，许申中书审察，与依合入远近权指射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169417_comment'></div>知县硬阙并无人愿就，过满见阙理监当人资任请受，仍不许不依常制奏辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169417_comment'></div>如此，则县道不至阙员，而微累之人免于留滞，可以责其后效矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169417_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈襄作《乞定审官东院条例状》<div id='poem_1169396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞定审官条例状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169396")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169396'>臣窃以审官东院之职，自少卿监知州军，至京朝官而下，不减三千馀员，注拟升改，所系非轻，事目尤众，宜其法式详备，乃可遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169396_comment'></div>而见用一司《编敕》，自熙宁八年颁行以来，中间续降节文，屡有冲改，已非旧文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169396_comment'></div>盖立法之初，失于简略，吏员既众，发遣不行，动多窒碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169396_comment'></div>条约事理，不能周尽，或轻重失当，于义未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169396_comment'></div>有司动须申明，士人时有诉述，裁决办理，上烦朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169396_comment'></div>臣自蒙恩领职，岁月颇久，考求利害，粗有条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169396_comment'></div>臣今欲乞将审官东院一司《敕》，依国子、司天监例，许从本院看详，删去烦文，补其阙略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169396_comment'></div>凡前后申明、所得朝旨，可立以为法者，并行编定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169396_comment'></div>其事理未尽未便者，并具奏陈，或申中书详酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169396_comment'></div>删成《审官东院令敕式》，庶几著为定法，可以久远施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169396_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈襄作《与富相公书》<div id='poem_1169515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与富相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169515")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169515'>某自河阳，得趋事于下，即蒙相公器遇，引荐置之文馆，夤缘以至近侍之官，区区之怀，未尝一得布露于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169515_comment'></div>尝谓士茍有志，壮而仕，老而休，必有以报称盛德之万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169515_comment'></div>伏自相公请还印绶，而某遂不获瞻望门下，于兹有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169515_comment'></div>愚陋阔疏，于时无补，今年六十，头白眼昏，膂力不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169515_comment'></div>道未有以加诸民，文未足以见于世，惟恐一旦功名泯灭，沦于犬马，以辱国士之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169515_comment'></div>虽然，今日之仕，观其去就之义，与其用舍之命，略可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169515_comment'></div>故自一二年来，其心汲汲，将勇退之计，而犹病未能者，生事未备故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169515_comment'></div>今者，不免强颜窃食于行列之间，俟其有备而后去，计亦不久于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169515_comment'></div>行与止系乎天，进与退存乎己，天其或者将以尧舜之道致其君、泽其民，则不可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169515_comment'></div>不然，则浩然而归，耕乎南海之滨，卒其所学，著书以见于后，亦足以无愧于门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169515_comment'></div>相公以为如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169515_comment'></div>惟公怜之，更赐教诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169515_comment'></div>某十八日即还都，谨此以代面布。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　陈襄提举司天监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年冬</a>　郊祀大礼，陈襄为礼仪吏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　陈襄作《依赦文举陈烈状》<div id='poem_1169384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>依赦文举陈烈状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169384")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169384'>准御史台牒，准熙宁十年九月七日敕，奉圣旨：一应内外官，待制以上，各于文臣内举才行堪任升擢官一员，令中书审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169384_comment'></div>如所举不谬，取旨随材用试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169384_comment'></div>即不得举已系带职及两府自己亲戚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169384_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1169384'>臣伏见前授安州司户参军、充国子监直讲陈烈，心仁气刚，才智卓越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169384_comment'></div>学圣人之言，而必践其行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169384_comment'></div>稽先王之法，而必适于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169384_comment'></div>博通群经，尤明于典礼之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169384_comment'></div>其为文章，渊源浩博，肆笔而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169384_comment'></div>求之宿儒，未有比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169384_comment'></div>庆历初，尝与乡贡，试于礼部，罢归田里，无复仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169384_comment'></div>安贫力学，积四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169384_comment'></div>著书数万言，未见其止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169384_comment'></div>仁宗朝，尝因近臣论荐，及本部监司长吏高其风节，数以名闻，累降召命，以学官起之，辞而不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169384_comment'></div>世以为洁身独行之士，是非知烈者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169384_comment'></div>烈之所学，皆孔孟之志，观其事业，足以有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169384_comment'></div>自以身载圣贤之道，不为茍进，可以礼致，而不可以利畜，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169384_comment'></div>伏思陛下享御以来，博延髦隽，得人之盛，跨越百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169384_comment'></div>如烈之贤，不为难致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169384_comment'></div>欲望陛下特以礼命，召至阙廷，赐对清间，亲降圣问，使陈二帝三王之术，六经四子之要，与夫当世之务，以著于篇，必有以上称陛下尊贤重德之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169384_comment'></div>今保举堪充清要，不次任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169384_comment'></div>如蒙朝廷擢用，后不如所举，臣甘坐面欺之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169384_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1169384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年春</a>　春，奉敕详定郊庙奉祀礼文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年夏</a>　决口塞，诏改新闭决河曹村埽曰灵平，遣陈襄为祭谢使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈襄作《详定礼文并制乐所定铜木尺度》一卷。<div id='poem_1169478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>详定礼文二<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>铜尺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169478")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169478'>皇祐五年五月，修制大乐所奉诏，以景表尺均通为皇祐中黍尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169478_comment'></div>大宋景祐二年岁次乙亥九月十二日依新黍定到律尺，每十黍为一寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169478_comment'></div>景祐丙子，皇帝诏臣逸、臣瑗准古法累秬黍以兴尺度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169478_comment'></div>景祐丙子，皇帝诏臣瑗准古法用上党秬黍累广成寸以兴尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169478_comment'></div>广监铸造臣刘保信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169478_comment'></div>修制大乐所皇祐二年闰十一月用乌圆小黍之广，累百满尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169478_comment'></div>修制大乐所皇祐二年闰十一月用乌圆中黍之广，累百满尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169478_comment'></div>修制大乐所皇祐二年闰十一月用乌圆大黍一黍之广，累百满尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169478_comment'></div>皇祐四年十一月内新置大乐所造到新定中黍连三铁尺石作使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169478_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1169478'>见管十五量尺名目：一、用尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169478_comment'></div>汉制刘歆铜斛尺、晋前尺并同后汉建武铜尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169478_comment'></div>二、晋田父玉尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（梁法尺同，比晋前尺一尺七厘。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169478_comment'></div>三、梁表尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（比晋前尺一尺二分二厘一毫有奇。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169478_comment'></div>四、汉官尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（比晋前尺一尺三分七毫。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169478_comment'></div>五、魏尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169478_comment'></div>六、晋后尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169478_comment'></div>七、后魏前尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（比晋前尺一尺一寸一分一厘。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169478_comment'></div>八、中尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（比晋前尺一尺一寸一分一厘。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169478_comment'></div>九、后尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169478_comment'></div>十、东魏后尺<span class='inlineComment2'>（比晋前尺一尺五寸八毫。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169478_comment'></div>十一、蔡邕铜籥尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169478_comment'></div>十二、宋氏尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169478_comment'></div>十三、万宝常水尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169478_comment'></div>十四、杂尺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169478_comment'></div>十五、梁朝俗间尺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1169478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169478'><span class='label'>按：</span>比晋前尺一尺七分三厘。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1169478_1'>⑴ 杜夔所用，比晋前尺一尺四分七厘。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169478_1'>⑵ 晋江东所用，比晋尺一尺六分二厘。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_1169478_1'>⑶ 隋开皇官尺、后周市尺并同，比晋前尺一尺二寸八分一厘。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1169478_1'>⑷ 后周王尺同，比晋前尺一尺一寸五分八厘。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1169478_1'>⑸ 钱乐之浑天仪尺、后周铁尺并同，比晋前尺一尺六分四厘。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_22_1169478_1'>⑹ 称其黄钟律当铁尺南吕倍声南吕黄钟之羽，故谓之水尺。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1169478_1'>⑺ 刘曜浑仪土圭尺也，比晋前尺一尺五寸。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169478_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈襄作《论乐劄子》<div id='poem_1169411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论乐劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169411")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169411'>臣谨看详：古者，先王用乐，皆有上下之节焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169411_comment'></div>《虞书》曰：「戛系鸣球，搏拊琴瑟以咏」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈襄作《祭天用乐劄子》<div id='poem_1169412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭天用乐劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169412")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169412'>臣谨按，《礼》：祀天以冬日至，取微阳洞开，天之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169412_comment'></div>兆于南郊，就阳位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169412_comment'></div>即地上之圜丘，因天事天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169412_comment'></div>燔燎而升烟，求阳以气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169412_comment'></div>玉奠苍璧，牲、币如其色，肖洪覆之自然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169412_comment'></div>乐用圜钟为宫，以其上应房、心，有天帝明堂之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169412_comment'></div>宫声三奏，角、徵、羽各一奏者，合阳奇之数，欲神之听之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169412_comment'></div>祭地以夏日至，取阴德潜萌，地之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169412_comment'></div>坎于北郊，从阴义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169412_comment'></div>就泽中方丘，因地事地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169412_comment'></div>瘗埋，顺其性之含藏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169412_comment'></div>方琮而黄币，仿形色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169412_comment'></div>乐用函钟为宫，以其生于未之气，未，坤位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169412_comment'></div>宫声与角、徵、羽各二奏者，合阴偶之数，所以八变，则地示出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169412_comment'></div>夫先王求神之意，可谓尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169412_comment'></div>以为天时者，乾坤因之而阖辟，阴阳系之而消长，鬼神亦由是而利用出入者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169412_comment'></div>故作大事必顺天时，既得其时，又择其位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169412_comment'></div>为高必因丘陵，为下必因川泽，以至于器币乐舞，至纤至悉，无不从其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169412_comment'></div>以此事神，则神无不飨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169412_comment'></div>汉元始间，不原《礼》意，附会《周官》大合乐之文，谓之合祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169412_comment'></div>复以正月三阳在下息，卦受《泰》，于是诹上辛之日，合祭天地于南郊，观其时位与夫器币乐舞之设，是徒寓地祇于啜食之列，而意不在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169412_comment'></div>后汉以正月上丁祠南郊，礼毕次北郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169412_comment'></div>下逮南齐，又以正月上辛祠昊天，次辛瘗后土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169412_comment'></div>虽得其位，不得其时，诚不至而礼不专，是亦主为礼天而发耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169412_comment'></div>窃有一證焉，《记》曰：「御同于长者，虽贰不辞，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1169412", 1169412, "Clauses/80/Comments/1")'>偶坐</span>不辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169412_comment'></div>郑氏曰：「盛馔不为已也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169412_comment'></div>王者事父孝，故事天明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169412_comment'></div>事母孝，故事地察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169412_comment'></div>岂可以后土富媪之灵，载物无疆之德，而事之仅如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1169412", 1169412, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>偶坐</span>之宾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169412_comment'></div>深恐柔祇未之享也。<div class='inline'
