id='poem_sentence_29_1169412_comment'></div>臣谨再详《仪注》，合祭天地于一坛之上，其为非礼明甚，固当改正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169412_comment'></div>然古今异宜，沿革殊致，三岁一郊，汉唐成宪，祖宗以来，莫能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169412_comment'></div>今罢合祭，则北郊惟使有司摄事，于理未安，谓宜以亲郊之岁，用夏日至先有事于方泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169412_comment'></div>盖祭者，荐其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169412_comment'></div>近人而亲者无如地，取材于地，故先祭以明亲亲之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169412_comment'></div>远人而尊者无如天，取法于天，故后祭以正尊尊之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169412_comment'></div>若青城，若张法驾，仪物一从简易，务称尚质之意，其扈卫锡与，可于郊赏数中豫给五分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169412_comment'></div>或量加特赐，系自上恩，所贵奉事天地，不失礼意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169412_comment'></div>惟朝廷财幸，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1169412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈襄撰《崇国夫人符氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1169574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169574?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崇国太夫人符氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169574")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169574'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169574'>夫人姓符氏，故尚书屯田郎中、赠给事中张公讳宗雅之妻，今宁州团练使、驸马都尉敦礼之母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169574_comment'></div>元丰元年六月二十二日以疾终于京师昭化坊之第，讣闻，三宫继遣中使奠，遗恩典周渥，追封崇国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169574_comment'></div>卫国长公主制齐衰服，朝夕哭临如礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169574_comment'></div>以其年九月二日，以一品礼祔葬于开封府祥符县开封乡马店村给事之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169574_comment'></div>按，符氏盖出于夏后氏之世，其初以蒲为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169574_comment'></div>晋征北大将军、广川郡公曰洪，与其孙坚，因改姓符氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169574_comment'></div>其后子孙居陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169574_comment'></div>夫人高祖讳彦卿，宛丘人也，仕五代之唐，太师、中书令、封魏王讳昭原嗣，为后周兴州刺史，开宝中入朝，从征太原，攻幽州，官至防御使，赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169574_comment'></div>子讳承祐，赠左武卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169574_comment'></div>武卫生讳惟忠，閤门副使、赠左屯卫上将军，即夫人之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169574_comment'></div>屯卫娶故燕国英惠大长公主女、长乐郡太君吴氏，实生夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169574_comment'></div>夫人幼而柔慧，长而端伟，事父母孝，称于族人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169574_comment'></div>尝侍屯卫读汉唐史，听而悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169574_comment'></div>屯卫曰：「此女喜事，非如贵戚家子，异日当配儒士，以光吾族」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169574_comment'></div>时给事方应科举，以文学游公卿，名称藉甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169574_comment'></div>屯卫乃以夫人妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169574_comment'></div>未几，给事由乡贡以说书赐进士出身，人始谓符公知人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169574_comment'></div>给事幼为小官，家甚贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169574_comment'></div>夫人居穷约中，甘心藜糗，怡然无不足色，而忘其世家贵侈之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169574_comment'></div>每归宁膝下，独以儒素自尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169574_comment'></div>屯卫益嘉其志，而知其器识之远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169574_comment'></div>夫人归，尝以不逮事舅姑为恨，春秋享祀，必躬治蘋藻，致其追奉之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169574_comment'></div>凡亲戚之孤遗匮乏者，则嫁娶而周给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169574_comment'></div>如给事之欲，虽力不足，竭衣珥所有以资之，无所爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169574_comment'></div>给事居常与士大夫议论，夫人多窃听之，退而品第其人物贤否，无不曲当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169574_comment'></div>尤喜闻政事与狱讼之疑难者，悉能区别情伪，裁之义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169574_comment'></div>故给事所治有异政，号为良吏，抑夫人之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169574_comment'></div>给事捐馆之日，家无馀赀，夫人节俭廑身，以赡亲族，外终襄事，入训诸孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169574_comment'></div>一日，召其子而谓之曰：「汝父以儒术起家，厥有馀构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169574_comment'></div>汝惟激昂自立，毋忝前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169574_comment'></div>菽水之须，吾自有处，非而曹忧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169574_comment'></div>诸子涕泣承教，相与愤悱，出从师学，遂得卒业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169574_comment'></div>既而第三子敦礼以文行预贡王府，士论翕然推重，天子知其名，选尚卫国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169574_comment'></div>入见禁中，训辞优厚，进封延安郡君，仍锡命服，当世荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169574_comment'></div>上方敦叙睦姻，深惟《春秋》正本之义，必自贵近者始，尝饬诸长公主，下嫁当行家人之礼，以见舅姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169574_comment'></div>卫国既归，祗循典则，庭闱温凊，闺阃肃雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169574_comment'></div>佥以夫人义训之效、积德之致然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169574_comment'></div>夫人慈俭庄淑，得之天性，其事人有礼，居家有法，待物有恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169574_comment'></div>内以辅佐君子，始终顺睦，无须臾之失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169574_comment'></div>外以亲厚姻族，承上遇下，皆得其驩心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169574_comment'></div>奉给事之丧，哀毁踰制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169574_comment'></div>服除，屏去簪珥，终身不事华靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169574_comment'></div>日课内典，求真如寂灭之趣，尤以杀生为深戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169574_comment'></div>常曰：「彼之怖死爱生，其情一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169574_comment'></div>如之何刲而食之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169574_comment'></div>忍人也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169574_comment'></div>遂不复鲜食，閒居清净，不见喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169574_comment'></div>奉养之具，不择丰约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169574_comment'></div>居富贵，不忘贫窭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169574_comment'></div>外物至，心无所撄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169574_comment'></div>殁之日，曲肱而逝，神色自若，可谓笃善令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169574_comment'></div>夫人笄而归给事四十二年，享年五十七，以给事恩封仁寿县君，以燕国甥赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169574_comment'></div>由延安郡君进封夫人，皆特恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169574_comment'></div>永嘉郡太君，吴郡太夫人，明堂南郊礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169574_comment'></div>至崇国，凡六封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169574_comment'></div>子三人：敦仁，守将作监主簿，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169574_comment'></div>敦义，山南东道节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169574_comment'></div>敦信，大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169574_comment'></div>皆有学行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169574_comment'></div>女五人：长适宗室右监门卫大将军、唐州团练使仲铣，封永安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169574_comment'></div>次适试将作监主簿燕琪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1169574_comment'></div>次适大理评事钱景历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1169574_comment'></div>次适光禄寺丞李士衮，先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1169574_comment'></div>其次继室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1169574_comment'></div>皆以妇道宜其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1169574_comment'></div>孙六人：秉渊，北京副使，卫国子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1169574_comment'></div>璹，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1169574_comment'></div>球，试将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1169574_comment'></div>璠、琮、玠，皆幼未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1169574_comment'></div>女孙十一人，长适右班殿直赵思行，馀未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1169574_comment'></div>都尉尝举进士，某时为考官，爱其文而荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1169574_comment'></div>久与游，闻其亲之贤，旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1169574_comment'></div>都尉又以伯父工部宗益状夫人之行请铭，宜为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1169574'>晋有符氏，曰洪与坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1169574_comment'></div>其后魏王，乃家于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1169574_comment'></div>皇祖二世，为我虎臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1169574_comment'></div>惟考屯卫，实生夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1169574_comment'></div>夫人贤慧，燕国之甥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1169574_comment'></div>志在图史，职司组紃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1169574_comment'></div>既归于家，降志安贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1169574_comment'></div>惠施姻族，孝荐蘩蘋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1169574_comment'></div>执夫之丧，居室辛勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1169574_comment'></div>诸孤卒业，令问日振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1169574_comment'></div>昂昂都尉，简帝之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1169574_comment'></div>王姬下降，天属联姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1169574_comment'></div>夫人入觐，帝有温言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1169574_comment'></div>启封锡服，福祉便蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1169574_comment'></div>谓宜遐寿，胡不畀纯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1169574_comment'></div>三宫遣奠，崇国疏恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1169574_comment'></div>礼备一品，真归九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1169574_comment'></div>德音不泯，昭此铭文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1169574_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈襄作《故太师中书令曾鲁公挽词》二首。<div id='poem_163565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故太师中书令曾鲁公挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163565")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163565'>天锡兴王佐，三朝秉化钧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163565'>平生清俭节，临老退閒身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163565'>赤舄荣封国，缁衣美世臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公之子继登二府。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163565'>永陪英庙享，千载德名新。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_163564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163564?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163564'>南台沙合后，元宰应时生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163564'>两控龙飞驭，三调宝鼎烹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163564'>筑山裴相乐，赐杖孔家荣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163564'>无复安舆出，儿孙衣䌽迎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163564'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年春</a>　春，陈襄兼判都省。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年冬</a>　冬，慈圣光献皇后崩，命陈襄为山陵卤簿使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　陈襄作《慈圣光献皇后挽词》二首。<div id='poem_163592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈圣光献太皇后挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163592")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163592'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163592'>天开华德嗣音徽，尝拥真人御殿闱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163592'>万国母仪坤积载，两朝圣嗣日光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163592'>羞笾忽弃参差荇，宝匣空馀浣濯衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163592'>从此昭陵原上路，又添遗老泣皇妃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163592'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163592_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_163591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163591?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163591'>庆寿蟠桃晓雾昏，忽闻笳鼓咽都门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163591'>宫闱有范遗文母，社稷无忧付圣孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163591'>四海心丧同祖妣，一封手诏易陵园。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163591'>君王孝感凌穹昊，未尽东朝欲报恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163591_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年3月</a>　陈襄卒于京师，将终，书“先圣先师”四字付其后。<br /></div>
-----end

浦城

<div class='label1' id='322bd7ccafee4aebbea6ab50ec2d2acb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("322bd7ccafee4aebbea6ab50ec2d2acb");'><span id='322bd7ccafee4aebbea6ab50ec2d2acb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1046')">1043-1046年</a>，27-30岁</div><div id='322bd7ccafee4aebbea6ab50ec2d2acb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年6月</a>　陈襄到浦城，有《谒庙祝文》<div id='poem_1169583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒庙祝文<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169583")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169583'>某伏闻县有官属到任，礼上讫，凡三日，始往拜诸庙之有灵德庇庥于邑人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169583_comment'></div>某职掌县簿，而且承长官阙，以躬临民，敢不夙戒，奔走承事，以告其至，明神降之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169583_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　陈襄作《祈雨》诗。<div id='poem_163617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祈雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163617")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_163617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163617'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163617'>庆历甲申岁，旱极忧民田。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163617'>农夫不得耕，相顾愁凶年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163617'>帝心恐民忧，诏遣祈山川。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163617'>郡国举祀典，斋戒陈豆笾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163617'>望祭复雩龙，祷之必精虔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_163617'>经旬杳无报，旱气增于前。<div id='poem_sentence_5_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_163617'>菑田扬飞尘，井谷无寸泉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_163617'>炎炎天地中，草木皆欲燃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_163617'>俗云有鳗鱼，灵异古所传。<div id='poem_sentence_8_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_163617'>太守顺民心，命驾而迎焉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_163617'>乐以钟鼓音，薰以沈檀烟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_163617'>倏惊西郊寒，霭霭离山巅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_163617'>急雨下滂沱，迅雷亦填填。<div id='poem_sentence_12_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_163617'>须臾畎亩盈，一境皆欣然。<div id='poem_sentence_13_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_163617'>始为穴中鱼，窃弄阴阳权。<div id='poem_sentence_14_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_163617'>山川岂无神，不能通于天。<div id='poem_sentence_15_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_163617'>蛟龙岂无灵，不能兴于渊。<div id='poem_sentence_16_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_163617'>有若赏罚柄，反使奸臣专。<div id='poem_sentence_17_163617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_163617'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_163617_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　陈襄作《祈雨祝文》<div id='poem_1169582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祈雨祝文<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169582")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169582'>某以王事，不能遍走山川神祇，谨择日用牲酒陈于龙坛之隅，置诸位，来尔诸庙之神以告之，神其听予言：今来自春徂夏，膏雨不时，川泽流竭，田苗将槁，人大恐怖，若无所依托，予亦不暇于饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169582_comment'></div>今农夫终岁勤劳于稼穑，惟天子租赋是供，亦惟尔神明粢醴是奉，尔尚庇庥于人，不可安以处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169582_comment'></div>县令既否德，不能活民，惟神活之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169582_comment'></div>亦惟尔世世于民，永有康食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169582_comment'></div>予虽比于罚，敢有词神，其降甘雨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1169582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　陈襄作《送章衡秀才序》<div id='poem_1169550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送章衡秀才序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169550")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169550'>予观天地人物，有可合之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169550_comment'></div>求合乎天下之方圆者，在知规矩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169550_comment'></div>求合乎天下之轻重者，在知权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169550_comment'></div>天地之道，难通也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169550_comment'></div>神明，难明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169550_comment'></div>万物之理，难齐一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169550_comment'></div>圣人尽心而诚焉，罔不通，罔不明，罔有不齐一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169550_comment'></div>圣人者，天地之合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169550_comment'></div>贤人者，求合乎圣人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169550_comment'></div>然则圣人不世出，乌乎合？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169550_comment'></div>曰：存则合乎人，亡则合乎经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169550_comment'></div>颜渊氏合乎人，孟、荀、扬、韩合乎经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169550_comment'></div>其事则同：好学以尽心，诚心以尽物，推物以尽理，明理以尽性，和性以尽神，如是而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169550_comment'></div>章衡子平，年弱冠，为予县学生，家居毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169550_comment'></div>祖母既老，一日挚书于门，告予归宁其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169550_comment'></div>义不可留，惜乎章生，吾不得以圣人之经为吾子合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169550_comment'></div>孔子没，六经之道不明于世，诸儒驳杂之说，纶纷乖错，周环天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169550_comment'></div>借使章生有贤，知人之材质焉，往而质语，吾以是为章生惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169550_comment'></div>章生汲汲求一官以为父母荣耶，则四方有馀师，其涂其径，其术甚易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169550_comment'></div>学将求合于圣人耶，则无近名，无躐学，无急于奔竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169550_comment'></div>发蒙乎四子，言行乎《诗》、《书》，性命乎《周易》，观法乎二《礼》，作事乎《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169550_comment'></div>富贵合乎是，贫贱合乎是，死生荣辱合乎是而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169550_comment'></div>或曰：「说经者多矣，焉攸从」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169550_comment'></div>曰：「乌用彼穿凿也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169550_comment'></div>诚至则经合，经至则圣人合，圣人至则天合矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169550_comment'></div>或曰：「焉知子是而信之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169550_comment'></div>曰：「质诸经，辅以四子，何疑而不信哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169550_comment'></div>章生求予言，予学徒也，不敢以教，重章生之材，往而无所合，姑以是为赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1169550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　陈襄作《答吕寺丞书》<div id='poem_1169505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答吕寺丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169505")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169505'>迩日伏惟起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169505_comment'></div>十一日，壮丁吴逸至，承赐书，陈列事序之始末，激之以仕进，要之以知己，至忠至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169505_comment'></div>某跪读之四五周，不能释手，窃有感发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169505_comment'></div>近世之士，轻义而重利，悲忧愉乐苟不系乎己，则虽父母兄弟有不得者，犹且彊为心颜，不肯一出意为之忧，其肯为他人谋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169505_comment'></div>某虽愚不肖，不敢妄有所图，然美君子之与人终始信厚能如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169505_comment'></div>虽然，某之心其所以为君子谋者，恐犹有未悉，故不敢不尽白焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169505_comment'></div>某凡在仕流间有与言语，窃自谓：吾师古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169505_comment'></div>至于古人之言行，非求知之，亦求信而蹈之者也，但学之有未及，行之有未至耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169505_comment'></div>然则干时进取之事，粗尝思之，虽未能脱合于正，然亦庶几无大过悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169505_comment'></div>昨者，太守谢侯与其从事皆相贤善，不自揆度，求为狱官，亦君子亲教诲而使之云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169505_comment'></div>始者尚不乐为，既而思之，无害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169505_comment'></div>司刑狱，亦吏之贱职，己为之，未为僭忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169505_comment'></div>又被举者得其人，有罪与否，举之者无赏罚，故举者不辞焉，遂以闻之，果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169505_comment'></div>若县令则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169505_comment'></div>国之政教始乎邑，民之生死系乎令，天子责公卿，选举得贤，为人父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169505_comment'></div>被举者茍非其人，不屑有罪，则连坐举者，不敢不慎择焉，非可求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169505_comment'></div>县令所治之土，小大与古诸侯之地相等，古者以郎官出宰百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169505_comment'></div>由也，圣门之高弟，材而勇者也，夫子则曰可以寄百里之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169505_comment'></div>如某则焉能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169505_comment'></div>前年至官，承其县令之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169505_comment'></div>始者，屡以言白于州，请辞不获，遂不得已为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169505_comment'></div>一年无所开明，听讼折狱，尽力而后止，忧劳成病，不能饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169505_comment'></div>士人百姓，但以一命从事，怜其如此，往往相谈以为己能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169505_comment'></div>退而反求诸心，配诸古人，固知怀惭负愧，无所容于天地，实不敢妄以为能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169505_comment'></div>夫动不可妄，妄而动，物不与也，虽与之，必有尤悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169505_comment'></div>《益》之上九曰：「莫益之，或击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169505_comment'></div>立心勿恒，凶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169505_comment'></div>谓不可益而益之，故或者必击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169505_comment'></div>天道有常数，君子有常心，数不过则天道无失其行，心不常则君子有致凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169505_comment'></div>子曰：「富而可求，虽执鞭之士，吾亦为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169505_comment'></div>如不可求，从吾所好」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169505_comment'></div>某岂敢废是言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169505_comment'></div>夫为贫而仕，充此一职，数口之家，可以无饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169505_comment'></div>今日之分，止可如此耳，鬼神临之，非敢妄说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169505_comment'></div>更将终始强学，以求成就其志，内可求于心，外可求于人，将席不暇暖，为之而不辞，岂在劝而后行，激而后为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169505_comment'></div>某是言也，未尝敢发，感君子之相爱，谨书之为谢，惟怜察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1169505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　陈襄作《黄殿丞书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　陈襄作《答黄殿丞书》<div id='poem_1169491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答黄殿丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169491")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169491'>某前月受所赐书一函，诚发于心，仁形于言，蔼蔼乎其言，雍雍乎其和，其大率称道小子，言尤过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169491_comment'></div>夫行古人之道，追慕圣贤之用心，在某愚钝，何能有此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169491_comment'></div>执事爱人乐善，闻而信之，不知采听之过欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169491_comment'></div>某虽愚无知，自到浦城二年，凡与士大夫相识，书辞往还，得其所操存，未有如执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169491_comment'></div>比得亲故书云：执事为政宽猛得中，昔人无与比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169491_comment'></div>初时未见颜色，用未敢决然信之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169491_comment'></div>及观书词，灼然见其心，于是信乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169491_comment'></div>吾父母邦之民，乐受福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169491_comment'></div>某尝谓侯官之民，粗识善恶，若得贤令，可以德化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169491_comment'></div>曩者，某人与某人，断断无他技，但能正行一事，公决一狱，民犹称之至今，耇老相传说以为故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169491_comment'></div>况执事今日之心，能尽己力行，一民一物，无不受赐，将来所收民言，宜如何多少哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169491_comment'></div>某官满即归田畴，愿与闻君子之风教，收拾补缀为之言，以与邻里乡党之人流传而歌之，俾吾民之不可忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169491_comment'></div>执事终始成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169491_comment'></div>春暄，伏惟起居多福，公暇善自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169491_comment'></div>谨奉书谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1169491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年10月</a>　陈襄建州浦城县主簿秩满。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a289c28223fc4f45aff26c78ed0896cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a289c28223fc4f45aff26c78ed0896cd");'><span id='a289c28223fc4f45aff26c78ed0896cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，36岁</div><div id='a289c28223fc4f45aff26c78ed0896cd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年春</a>　春，陈襄过浦城，作《留题南峰寺》<div id='poem_163569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇祐四年春重到浦城县南峰寺因怀旧游</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163569")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163569'>重到南峰寺，寻思九日游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163569'>黄花何处去，白雪有谁留<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163569'>薄宦三千里，流光四十秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163569'>归来见诸子，林下好相求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163569'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_163569'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_163569_0'>⑴ 自注：某昔年官浦城，重阳日宴县学诸生二百人于此寺，作赋歌诗。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_163569_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
仙居
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cdc06324d3e945f58e68dee69f35b33a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdc06324d3e945f58e68dee69f35b33a");'><span id='cdc06324d3e945f58e68dee69f35b33a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1051')">1047-1051年</a>，31-35岁</div><div id='cdc06324d3e945f58e68dee69f35b33a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　陈襄以部使者举为台州仙居县令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　陈襄作《仙居劝谕文》<div id='poem_1169481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仙居劝学文</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169481")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169481'>咨汝邑父老：夫人之为善，莫善于读书为学，学然后知礼义孝悌之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169481_comment'></div>故一子为学，则父母有养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169481_comment'></div>一弟为学，则兄姊有爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169481_comment'></div>一家为学，则宗族和睦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169481_comment'></div>一乡为学，则闾里康宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169481_comment'></div>一邑为学，则风俗美厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169481_comment'></div>虽有恶人，将变而为善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169481_comment'></div>今天子三年一选士，虽山野贫贱之家所生子弟，茍有文学，必赐科名，身享富贵，家门光宠，户无徭役，休荫子弟，岂不为盛事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169481_comment'></div>予自到任以来，居常悯汝邑民不识为学，父子兄弟不相孝友，乡党邻里不相存恤，其心汲汲，惟争财竞利为事，以至身冒刑宪，鞭箠流血而不知止，予甚哀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169481_comment'></div>奈奉天子诏条，不可私恕，每刑一身，若伤肤发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169481_comment'></div>而汝邑民不知予心，乃相扇炽，搆讼成狱，自以为能使予日不得食，夜不得寝，欲与革弊，略不能改，是诚何心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169481_comment'></div>虽然，非汝百姓之乐于此也，盖不知读书之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169481_comment'></div>前年曾有文书告谕汝乡民，令遣子弟入学，于今二年矣，何其无人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169481_comment'></div>古者，十室之邑，必有忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169481_comment'></div>今百里之邑，良民子弟不少，其间岂无聪明瑰茂朴美之器，可使为公卿者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169481_comment'></div>然而不使之为学，真可惜也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169481_comment'></div>今汝父老归告其子弟，远令来学，予其择明师而教诲之，庶几有成，如前所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169481_comment'></div>予明年十二月官满即去，汝父老其听予言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　陈襄作《谢关郎中书》<div id='poem_1169514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢关郎中书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169514")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169514'>某愚，不习于法，伏蒙执事恕其不逮，三舍其过，知所幸，诚惶诚恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169514_comment'></div>《书》曰：「宥过无大」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169514_comment'></div>谓人之过失，非有其故，则当宽于常刑，不宜大之，是犹未免于无罚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169514_comment'></div>《蒙》之初六，居蒙之始，九二临之，则发其蒙，再三不解，至于终蒙，上则击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169514_comment'></div>所宜罚而弗罚，当所可击而弗击，则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169514_comment'></div>圣人之法，又可过乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169514_comment'></div>惟大人者不然，当罚之无罚也，当击之无击也，处之有义，行之有道，圣人何过焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169514_comment'></div>不知义者，不能如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169514_comment'></div>今有人之子，居童蒙未开之时，有所不逮，为之父母者，不直怒而谴之，隐忍而全之者，所以待于后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169514_comment'></div>至于士屯蒙未开，有所不逮，为之长者，岂得直怒而谴之，不隐忍而全之，而无所待于后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169514_comment'></div>然则待于子之贤者，不过立身扬名以显父母，而能保其祭祀焉尔，一身之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169514_comment'></div>待于士之贤者，有能推仁致义，以利天下，为生民之福，天下之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169514_comment'></div>大人为义，不亦尚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169514_comment'></div>夫舍其小而存其大，不执一以废于百，能知是者，其义可胜道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169514_comment'></div>某十岁而学孔子之道，行之二十有三年，庶几夙夜至其所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169514_comment'></div>今也，困于蒙昧有所不逮之时，使得曲而全之，道未丧，有所用于天下，则执事之义何如其小大也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169514_comment'></div>谨具书诣门下致谢<span class='inlineComment2'>（《古灵先生文集》卷八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169514_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1169514'>时：库本作「义」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　陈襄作《劝学文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　陈襄作《天台山习养瀑记》<div id='poem_1169563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天台山习养瀑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169563")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169563'>夫水有君子之道二，其大焉者，《易》曰「习坎有孚」，言其用焉者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169563_comment'></div>孔子曰「水哉水哉」，言其本焉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169563_comment'></div>圣人有忧患，言能行天下之险者，莫善于水，故文王取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169563_comment'></div>君子之道，犹源泉之有积，不可以不养也，故孔子取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169563_comment'></div>予游天台山，始至福圣观观瀑，寻而上观三井，涉潭洞，历桐柏观，登琼台，下龙湫，顾其飞流壮猛，出高入下，不见所困，竟又不得其源焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169563_comment'></div>其畜之也不匮，其施之也不困，非善习险而固有本者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169563_comment'></div>宜名其前曰习养之瀑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169563_comment'></div>县令石牧之、进士余京与吾勉焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169563_comment'></div>其馀嵓峰之秀，林麓之好，真神人所居，吾不能言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1169563_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　陈襄作《天台县孔子庙记》<div id='poem_1169564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天台县孔子庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169564")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169564'>孔子，圣人之大备者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169564_comment'></div>使得百里之国，以为政于天下，虽尧舜不可及已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169564_comment'></div>为天子者，不以有己，听命以治其天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169564_comment'></div>为诸侯者，不以有己，听命以治其国，则必期月而为东周矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169564_comment'></div>惜乎天民之不遇，命也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169564_comment'></div>自唐以来，天下郡县始立孔子庙，追尊王爵，春秋释奠，天子以下皆执弟子礼，世以为尊用孔子之道，如是岂其然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169564_comment'></div>生而有盛德于民，死以祭礼报之，如曰尊用其道，则未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169564_comment'></div>天下之文弊久矣，自周至于今，宜黜浮伪，尚忠实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169564_comment'></div>百物或有失职者，宜正名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169564_comment'></div>王泽或有壅滞者，宜任大臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169564_comment'></div>远近官政或有冗滥者，宜能官人，贤者以政，不贤者以禄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169564_comment'></div>教或有未至者，宜兴学校，隆师儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169564_comment'></div>礼或有未修者，宜教民冠昏丧祭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169564_comment'></div>乐或有未作者，宜考五声十二律，放郑卫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169564_comment'></div>豪杰或有未出者，宜拔贤才，举逸民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169564_comment'></div>鳏寡孤独或有未养者，宜弛力舍禁，授田以制，取财以节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169564_comment'></div>民之蠹或有未去者，宜黜佛老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169564_comment'></div>戎狄之患或有未备者，宜足兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169564_comment'></div>孔子之道，用必先于此数者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169564_comment'></div>夫能立庙以守其祭祀，尚未为得礼者，而况于用乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169564_comment'></div>天台县有孔子庙不修，县令石牧之始至，岁十月相县之城南隅，大作新庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169564_comment'></div>屋总六十有二楹，先树正殿，塑孔子南向，左右十哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169564_comment'></div>曾子自馀弟子六十有一人，与诸儒传经者二十有一人，皆图诸壁间，皆以其所追爵等降，如周之服冕圭璧，惟孟轲、荀卿、扬雄、韩愈氏服儒服焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169564_comment'></div>中树讲堂，图古之儒服、礼乐之器于其两壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169564_comment'></div>后又设学舍，师生讲习，咸有位序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169564_comment'></div>祭器在西房，庖厨在东房，周回门廊，环以墙宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169564_comment'></div>又考古器，作笾豆、簠簋、樽罍、俎爵之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169564_comment'></div>十二月庙成，明年春秋释奠，入而行礼，生徒与事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169564_comment'></div>品物如制，像图尊严，笾俎新嘉，神明燕喜，人物观化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169564_comment'></div>先，兹邑民不识儒学，又故庙湫隘，与民杂居，侮慢不尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169564_comment'></div>至是耳目闻觉，始有学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169564_comment'></div>嗟乎，石君可谓有志矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169564_comment'></div>区区小邑，而能为孔子立庙，制度以礼，春秋以时祀之，俾民不忘，是已无愧于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169564_comment'></div>如其欲用孔子，则天也，非力之所能及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169564_comment'></div>天其不欲以斯道觉斯民也，则其已矣乎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169564_comment'></div>如欲以斯道觉斯民也，石君之志，其必有遇矣！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1169564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　陈襄作《和郑闳中仙居》诗12首。<div id='poem_163548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和郑闳中仙居十一首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163548")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163548'>我爱仙居好，临民必以诚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163548'>簿书无日暇，狱讼积年生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163548'>百疾求箴补，千钧待准平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163548'>嗟予不如古，斯道未能宏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_163548'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_163548_0'>⑴ 自注：予始至，邑豪有以债负凭折细民田土者，迹验分明，予治而归之。或有年深而无稽者，亦妄词讼，三年分户二千。凡有产而无业，积年空纳其租，许其还主者，不可胜数。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_163548_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_163547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163547?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><br id='poem_sentence_1_163547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163547'>喜有纲条立，惭无教令颁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163547'>三年忧且病，王事岂能閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163547'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163547_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_163546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163546?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163546'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163546'>我爱仙居好，园池日退居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163546'>草树通樵采<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，桑麻有老锄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163613'>三年邑未化，官满意彷徨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163613'></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_163613_0'>⑵ 自注：公暇，每有童子十数人至堂上，教授经书或试之诗。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_163613_0'>⑶ 自注：因孔子庙后修起学舍，买三家之地，以广其基。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_163613_0'>⑷ 自注：予每出行诸乡，遇有小学则下，以观童子。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_163613_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_163543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_163543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_163542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163542?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163542'>我爱仙居好，家居十数人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_163541_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_163540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163540?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_163612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163612?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_3_163612'>一年人已信，感激谢张弧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　陈襄改秘书省著作佐郎、知孟州河阳县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　陈襄作《怀友人陈烈》<div id='poem_163522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀友人陈烈</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163522")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163522'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163522'>思君苦节直艰难，四十穷经草野间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163522'>文为周衰能力救，礼遭秦祸欲重删<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163522'>时无正说非杨墨，天与多才继孔颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163522'>吾主聘贤方仄席，好将书币起东山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163522'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_163522'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_163522_0'>⑴ 自注：烈自庆历初下第退居东山，潜心礼书已十年矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_163522_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　陈襄作《祭仙孙五郎文》<div id='poem_1169581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭仙孙五郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169581")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169581'>呜呼仙孙，生汝七十日，未熟汝面，汝遽亡耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169581_comment'></div>黄岩之别，舟中抱汝，不觉出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169581_comment'></div>深知汝幼，不利远行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169581_comment'></div>过在父母，复将谁冤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169581_comment'></div>吾在京师，闻汝之归，举家疾疫，十死四五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169581_comment'></div>凡十月馀日，不得汝娘一书，心亦惊忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169581_comment'></div>然又闻汝子母康宁，不复省察，岂宜汝遽如此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169581_comment'></div>朋友家人，具知汝事，讳不吾言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169581_comment'></div>故吾今日之心，犹望望然欲即见汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169581_comment'></div>梁益来汝娘书，又讳不言及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169581_comment'></div>得季甫先生书，始知汝诚亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169581_comment'></div>呜呼仙孙，汝负吾耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169581_comment'></div>吾朋友四五人，皆忧惊晚娶，未有嗣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169581_comment'></div>吾又多病，不保久长，及汝之生，始安吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169581_comment'></div>故吾日夕冀汝长立，上奉汝先翁之祀，下以继吾之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169581_comment'></div>岂知汝遽如此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169581_comment'></div>汝将不为吾儿，则不如勿生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169581_comment'></div>生既不幸而夭，亦当使吾见而诀之，曷为使吾终身置汝不足于心也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169581_comment'></div>吾尝与汝娘言：人之于骨肉，无老幼，生则相养，死当葬埋，封识使之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169581_comment'></div>闻汝亡时，娘亦不得闻知，未知置汝于何所耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169581_comment'></div>汝身幸存，是天锡吾儿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169581_comment'></div>汝身不存，吾生何乐也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169581_comment'></div>吾无意于世久矣，思汝先亡翁，与二先亡婆，洎汝世母，皆早世，坟墓未安，常欲买一山，族而葬之，舍官，庐其旁，以老吾身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169581_comment'></div>今汝又亡，吾志愈决矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169581_comment'></div>使吾今日即居显官，享丰禄，以茍富贵，若吾亲与吾子血肉在土，于吾何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169581_comment'></div>虽然，吾今日之力，未能图之，尚须任满河阳，继入远宦，可六七年，汝身幸存，即图南归，卜庐墓事，瘗汝于亡翁之侧，安汝于吾庐之旁，吾心始安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169581_comment'></div>呜呼仙孙，恨汝未知吾言，汝知吾心之苦否也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169581_comment'></div>今遣梁益归，请汝娘浇酒瘗吾文于汝旁，以安汝魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169581_comment'></div>汝能知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169581_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1169581_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f8a88bb7eb4240ca958a07e0c4a316b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f8a88bb7eb4240ca958a07e0c4a316b5");'><span id='f8a88bb7eb4240ca958a07e0c4a316b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>，46岁</div><div id='f8a88bb7eb4240ca958a07e0c4a316b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　陈襄作《请顾临秘校主学书》<div id='poem_1169500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州请顾临秘校主学书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169500")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169500'>某窃以东南之学，废而不振也已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169500_comment'></div>安定先生之去吴兴，盖十馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169500_comment'></div>天下学者之兴，较之当时，固已寖盛，而东南之士，又常倍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169500_comment'></div>然而魁奇特起之才，礼乐恺悌之风，反不如吴兴昔时之盛，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169500_comment'></div>岂非庠序之教，所由废兴也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169500_comment'></div>某之不肖，领郡于兹，虽不敢以斯道为己任，然常患近世之士，溺于章句之学，而不知先王礼义之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169500_comment'></div>上自王公，下逮士人，其取人也，莫不以善辞章者为能，守经行者为迂阔，而士之荣辱，亦从而应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169500_comment'></div>以是天下之士习非舍是，固已涂瞆其耳目，而莫之能正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169500_comment'></div>某自涖事以来，惟日孜孜以兴学养士为先务，以明经笃行为首选，其心如是，直将以待夫有志之士焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169500_comment'></div>彼州人之子弟，与夫四方之学者，轻千里而至，其亦有望于兹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169500_comment'></div>虽然，德薄任重，知不足以独当其责，思得先生老成之士为之表率而未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169500_comment'></div>伏惟足下才足以宰制于人，义足以矫厉于时，其所为文，又有以惊动时人之耳目，今将表一学之生徒，而教之以德行道艺之术，所宜无让也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169500_comment'></div>谨遣诸生，躬诣门下以请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169500_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
淮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f8894504357a4ae7a30b9f98b7ec68b4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f8894504357a4ae7a30b9f98b7ec68b4");'><span id='f8894504357a4ae7a30b9f98b7ec68b4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>，55岁</div><div id='f8894504357a4ae7a30b9f98b7ec68b4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年冬</a>　冬，陈襄出知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　陈襄作《到陈谢富相公启》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d031b39c95d44532816ac420ec14bbe5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d031b39c95d44532816ac420ec14bbe5");'><span id='d031b39c95d44532816ac420ec14bbe5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1075')">1074-1075年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='d031b39c95d44532816ac420ec14bbe5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　陈襄作《陈州谢到任表》<div id='poem_1169354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169354")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169354'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169354'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，差知陈州军州事，已于今月十九日到任，礼上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169354_comment'></div>治剧非长，偶逭旷官之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169354_comment'></div>均恩特厚，未遗旅力之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169354_comment'></div>况近屏之素优，实愚臣之旧治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169354_comment'></div>已颁新令，再涖属民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169354_comment'></div>居逸而休，冒荣以惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169354_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169354_comment'></div>伏念臣师于古学，起自海滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169354_comment'></div>才不逮人，利常居于众后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169354_comment'></div>身惟徇道，思或得于时中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169354_comment'></div>不图明哲之知，滥与清华之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169354_comment'></div>一违禁掖，三易名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169354_comment'></div>勉究吏文，几殚心气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169354_comment'></div>终乏殊尤之效，重叨偃息之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169354_comment'></div>岁未越于再期，民犹知于旧尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169354_comment'></div>逋逃稍去，旄倪相欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169354_comment'></div>负弩道旁，尚存故吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169354_comment'></div>憩棠郊外，仅有遗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169354_comment'></div>宜在此时，益修前政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169354_comment'></div>富庶未加，则务劝相而无扰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169354_comment'></div>孝弟未化，则思驯致之有方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169354_comment'></div>庶几黾勉于三年，可使阜安于百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169354_comment'></div>斯盖伏遇皇帝陛下，规恢大业，总揽群英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169354_comment'></div>谓耳目之臣，不使远离于王室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169354_comment'></div>念本根之治，必先取重于辅藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169354_comment'></div>致兹孤拙之踪，常与品题之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169354_comment'></div>臣敢不祗循圣训，益励官箴，宽布化条，勤恤民隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169354_comment'></div>中畿甚迩，惟依天日之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169354_comment'></div>旧俗犹淳，愿致国风之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169354_comment'></div>庶少裨于鸿造，期无负于赤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169354_comment'></div>臣无任戴天荷圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169354_comment'></div>谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169354_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1169354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　陈襄作《自杭之宋过永乐院留题》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在本年，地点在自杭之宋途中，不能确知。）</span><div id='poem_163635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熙宁七年八月望日自杭之宋过永乐院观承天佛日广慧洎永乐四老上堂因而留题</a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163635")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_163635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163635'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163635'>雷音一振绝微言，末学方知祖道尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163635'>莫讶师僧无见处，人人俱解句中玄<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作论）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163635'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_163635_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　陈襄作《颍州府学释奠勉童子》<div id='poem_163492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍州府学释奠先圣郡中童子亦来拜谒以诗勉之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163492")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_163492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163492'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163492'>蔼蔼青衿子，来修谒庙仪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163492'>怜他眉宇秀，中有起家儿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163492'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_163492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　陈襄作《颍川赏花》诗二首。<div id='poem_163491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍川赏花二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163491")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_163491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163491'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163491'>閒入郊园驻隼旟，百花红紫万千株。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163491'>如何春意多风雨，不惜漫天锦绣铺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163491'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_163491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_163490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163490?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_163490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163490'>千骑重来此建旟，新年花发旧年株。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163490'>东皇应是怜孤宦，十里全归锦帐铺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163490'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_163490_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb2a062ec9b34b38b1603b6d0dd5fd8f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb2a062ec9b34b38b1603b6d0dd5fd8f");'><span id='eb2a062ec9b34b38b1603b6d0dd5fd8f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1074')">1072-1074年</a>，56-58岁</div><div id='eb2a062ec9b34b38b1603b6d0dd5fd8f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年秋</a>　秋，陈襄移知杭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　陈襄作《劝学文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　陈襄作《夫人吴氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1169568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人吴氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169568")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169568'>夫人姓吴氏，世为钱塘人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169568_comment'></div>大父事吴越王，至将相，归朝为刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169568_comment'></div>考讳充，右侍禁、湖州兵马监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169568_comment'></div>妣钱氏，工部侍郎、赠刑部尚书讳昱之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169568_comment'></div>夫人于伦次最季，年十岁而妣钱氏亡，诸兄以故时器服奁具厚自殖，夫人独不顾之，养侍禁谨甚，而事其兄以顺，卒相视欢然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169568_comment'></div>及侍禁弃舍馆，贫敝零丁，无所归，他人视之，若不胜其忧者，夫人能自刻削，习为俭薄，不以困约有所不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169568_comment'></div>礼宾副使、知凤州钱公讳绛之室南宫县君吴氏，盖夫人之族也，念其子大理寺丞讳访之贤，难所以配者，习知夫人所为，隆爱之，遂以为大理君之配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169568_comment'></div>夫人之归，大理君方恓恓簿领，顾其家枵然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169568_comment'></div>南宫与所生宣氏皆无恙，夫人事之能尽，莫有间言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169568_comment'></div>二人交称于其族人曰：「吾老矣，非此妇不能以安我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169568_comment'></div>夫人始三十七岁，而大理君早世，家益困，诸孤累然，二子长文、长卿尚稚，未有所识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169568_comment'></div>夫人攻苦食淡，躬自诲之，损资币使就学，暮归，必考其业，而验其记诵之精否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169568_comment'></div>平居督戒，不得妄与人游，常所往来，必一时闻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169568_comment'></div>每客至，夫人从户窥之，信贤欤，为亲具酒食，数延见不厌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169568_comment'></div>一有非是，立诫以绝，故二子稍长，皆好学而文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169568_comment'></div>吴中多以夫人教子为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169568_comment'></div>其后长卿以主簿侍夫人之官，所俸给至薄，常以甘毳不备为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169568_comment'></div>夫人谕之曰：「节俭以立名，而职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169568_comment'></div>顾吾何累焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169568_comment'></div>在吴门，闻安定先生之贤，四方之士从之游者多为望人，其主教太学也，长卿适求调于京师，夫人实命从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169568_comment'></div>及其官久不遂，同时进士往往见进用且显矣，族属悉以为夫人憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169568_comment'></div>夫人笑且言曰：「士之穷达有命，恃吾有以待之，速进何慕耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169568_comment'></div>平生自奉寡约，华簪侈珥，不以动其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169568_comment'></div>族人之来者，必厚遇之，虽历年不倦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169568_comment'></div>视其空无能振之，亦不为后日毫发计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169568_comment'></div>故其子阅官且二十年矣，其惫滋甚，夫人尚敝衣恶食，自如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169568_comment'></div>其治家事，委曲皆有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169568_comment'></div>处用度，不肯辄过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169568_comment'></div>而于岁时祭祀，必尽其恭严，治果蔬鱼肉，常身先之，不自其手不以祭，故其子妇不懈益恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169568_comment'></div>天资慈祥，不忤物，其下有所忤己，即置之，未尝辄怀忮恨于其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169568_comment'></div>熙宁三年十月三十日以疾终，享年六十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169568_comment'></div>子七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169568_comment'></div>三男：长曰长文，屡荐于有司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169568_comment'></div>次曰长卿，秘书省著作佐郎、御史台主簿、枢密院编修经武要略兼删定诸房例册；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169568_comment'></div>次曰长倩，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169568_comment'></div>四女：长适舒州望江县令姚琪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169568_comment'></div>次适西安詹玠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169568_comment'></div>次适剑南西川节度推官、知桂州永宁县事贾逢，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169568_comment'></div>次适丹阳邵褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169568_comment'></div>孙男五人，曰：轙、辙、轵、轸，一尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169568_comment'></div>孙女六人，长适太常寺奉礼郎魏漳，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169568_comment'></div>以五年二月庚申，合大理君之丧，葬润州丹徒县崇德乡鸿鹄山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169568_comment'></div>前事，长卿以屯田员外郎长乐孙奕之状，再拜泣血问铭于予曰：「吾母劬劳焘后，其行事可考，不诬如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169568_comment'></div>愿先生赐之铭，于以图其传于不朽，可不可耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169568_comment'></div>予以为，昔者先王之泽存，所以致治于天下者，必起于闺门之隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169568_comment'></div>至其教明俗成，则《兔罝》之武夫犹好德，而《汝坟》之妇人知勉君子以正，盖其法度之盛，有以致然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169568_comment'></div>及先王之泽亡，而室家之治，槩无法以成之，故妇人女子之泯然，无足怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169568_comment'></div>自非资适高明、操行之特立，其能终止于礼义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169568_comment'></div>以是论之，则夫人之德贤于人远矣，此法之所宜铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169568_comment'></div>遂受而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169568_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1169568'>噫嗟夫人，行则仁兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169568_comment'></div>两承而欢，极志养兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169568_comment'></div>示子义荣，德高明兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169568_comment'></div>不悯阨穷，能顺命兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169568_comment'></div>周无振乏，广睦族兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169568_comment'></div>败衣恶食，其乐全兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169568_comment'></div>采蘋为羞，后所循兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169568_comment'></div>忤己不校，恩逮下兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169568_comment'></div>谓当难老，将福禄兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169568_comment'></div>理有芒昧，止此极兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169568_comment'></div>我知其贤，宜始风兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1169568_comment'></div>作为铭诗，永厥声兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1169568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年10月</a>　陈襄作《饯送钱塘贡士登彼公堂》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年10月</a>　陈襄作《题忠定张公书后》<div id='poem_1169552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题忠定张公书后<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_1169552")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169552'>忠定公生有大节，人至于今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169552_comment'></div>公之曾孙尧夫为宛丘令，出公墨迹二本，予读久之，嗟慕无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169552_comment'></div>况功行伟卓，传于后人口者，宜其不忘也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1169552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　陈襄在杭州修钱塘六井。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年春</a>　春，钱塘六井迄工，苏轼为之作记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　陈襄作《和子瞻吉祥冬日牡丹》诗三首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　陈襄作《和子瞻沿牒京口忆西湖寒食》<div id='poem_163530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和子瞻沿牒京口忆西湖寒食出游见寄二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34427, "北宋", "陈襄", "poem_title_163530")'>陈襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163530'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163530'>乞得湖山养病身，花时曾共忆行春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163530'>嘤鸣幽鸟还迁木，觱沸清泉复采芹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163530'>皂盖寻芳丘有李，䌽楼观戏巷无人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163530'>锦袍公子归何晚，独念沟中菜色民<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163530'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_163530'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_163530_0'>⑴ 自注：时子瞻沿漕檄赈济常、润饥民。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_163530_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_163529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/163529?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_163529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_163529'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_163529'>春阴漠漠燕飞飞，可惜春光与子违。<div id='poem_sentence_0_163529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_163529'>半岭烟霞红旆入，满湖风月画船归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_163529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_163529'>缑笙一阕人何在，辽鹤重来事已非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_163529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_163529'>犹忆去年题别处，鸟啼花落客沾衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_163529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_163529'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_163529_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　陈襄移应天府留守，未至，复移知陈州。<br /></div>
-----end
